2017-12-31 20:48:08
Pritam Guha
8111591
3.0
I have heard about the legendary OlyPub in Park Street for many a year now and decided that the final day of 2017 was an appropriate day to give the place a visit. The restaurant is located between The Park and McDonald's in Park Street. We went at around 1 o'clock in the afternoon and hence did not have to wait for finding a seat. The place does have an average amount of seating arrangement which is not too large, nor too small. We were a group of three friends. Majority of the seats were for groups of 4 or more and I did not notice any for a couple of people or so. The first thing which left an impression in me was "Biff Steak" in their menu which I could not accept as OlyPub is a legendary dining place. The booze was quite cheap over here but I was disappointed on not getting Budweiser. So, we all settled for a Carlsberg Elephant each. We decided to try out the Beef Steak and Chicken Ala Kiev which is quite synonymous with this place. The Beef Steak is okayish and is not very spectacular. But I loved the Chicken Ala Kiev and may give another visit just to have this. It was too good and it is fair to say I haven't tasted a better one. I left OlyPub with the final impression of having to pay an extra Rs. 100 due to the negligence of the management which we later rectified, upon which the staff apologized. I hope this was just a one-off day at the legendary restaurant.

One of the signature places of Park Street, this pub is famous for serving drinks and food at affordable prices. It used to be an excellent place to hang out with friends and have a chit-chat over a few pegs.

I've been to this place a couple of times but honestly saying, it has lost its old charm and service. Their quality of food has degraded too! You hardly get good choices of drinks and almost always you'll have to end up ordering the brand you don't like.

Last time we went there, like always we had the famous Beef Steak! But the meat was so hard! Ordered beer, Fish Cutlet and Grilled Fish too. The fish items were tasty. Since we were still feeling hungry, we ordered Tandoori Chicken too.

The staffs need to be more courteous. They do not behave well or even answer properly. The ambiance has degraded too. But this place still holds lots of memories with friends.

Cheers to food! Cheers to life!

2017-11-09 21:22:42
Avra Paul
33275092
2.0
This place has ground and level one sitting interior is normal i mean nothing so impressive.
This place is perfect for drinks. The crowd here is also well behaved. Please don't try their food items. We ordered chicken ala olypub and paneer tikka. I really wish I could abuse the chef like the "NAGARPALIKA" guy. Yes the food was horrible. I knew I shouldn't have expected a lot from this place considering we were not looking for fine dining. Parking is available but at your own risk, someone stole my bike's mirrors last time I visited this place and both the police and parking ticket collector denied that the mirrors were stolen. So be a bit cautious and try to park your vehicles near any stores' cctv cams. It's just a great place to have drinks. "Daaru sasta milta hai bhai aur kya chahiye".

##

2017-11-09 18:09:29
Chaotic_foodie
1526503
3.5
Sheer nostalgia! One of the oldest pubs of Kolkata, still filled with that same ineffable aura. Olypub is the ultimate place for 'happy dining'. Though crowded most of the times, their delivery is prompt. Prices are reasonable too. And the ambiance, as I've already said bears that quaint vintage charm.

Tried out their renowned Chicken Ala Kiev which consisted two chicken pieces accompanied with mashed potatoes and peas. Also I tried their Butter Nan and Chicken Butter Masala. It tasted quite okay but I found it too much oily. But the Chicken Ala Olypub was the best choice and I personally liked it way more than Ala Kiev.

According to me, Olypub is the best place for Continental dishes as they are great in taste and the price surge is low.

Okay. :)

2017-11-05 08:31:09
Devarsi Ghosh
6897161
3.5
I have been visiting Olypub since 2010 when I first got into college which was at Park Street and hence, my initiation into alcohol obviously had to begin at Oly, the haven for drinkers in Central Kolkata. To be honest, I liked Oly before the renovation. It's not because everything was cheaper or you could smoke inside Oly, that's not it. The reason I say this is because the food has become bloody terrible. I haven't had issues with alcohol. Yes, alcohol pricing is a bit on the higher side if you compare it with the average pricing of all Kolkata dive bars.¬†But, anybody who goes to Oly usually goes for the ambience and the charm which usually appeals to those who have grown up with it, such as me.

For instance, I know, on any given day, I could go to a better joint than Oly, but I stick to Oly because it's familiar. It has a lived-in quality. And also, because they make amazing beef steak. There's no option to dictate how you want the beef to be cooked; it will always come well-done. Actually, the beef steak, today, is the only good thing to eat at Oly. That's the only thing I'd suggest one to have at Oly.

1.5
I was with a friend who visited kolkata for the first time and on the very first day we went to park street.
We checked in around 1 pm and there was no one around except some waiters. Even if there were no customers it took them 10 minutes to come to our table serve water.
Oh god someone noticed us ...we were happy....
Waiter: kya chahiye?
Me:pehle pani....
Waiter too another 10 minutes to come with water.
Me: one bira strong and one carlsberg stong
Waiter: khali tuborg strong,kingfisher strong and breezer hai
Me and my friend were thinking what to order he left the table and stood against the wall behind us. Just after 30 secs he vanished and we were waiting for another 10 mins to give order.
Me: ek tuborg strong and breezer
In the mean time we ordered mutton sheekh kebab,chicken sheekh kebab and prawn chilli.
Coming to food it was all horrible.
All the kebabs were full of cheap quality bread crumbs. They were hard ,dry and tasteless. Took one bite and told him to pack those sticks(they are not even qualified to be called kebabs)
Prawn chilli was greasy and too much oily.
Small prawn coated with lot of flour and corn flour and fried with bad oil .
Only good thing was the complementary "chanachur".
So at the end i did not regret coming oly pub although i was staying in kolkata since 5 years.

Before you go to Olypub, you must know what to expect. It has been famous for it's steak and other continental dishes. Although service can always be improved upon, and some more enthusiasm on part of the waiters could be added. So if you are heading there, put your hat aside, and just sit and enjoy your drink and the steak.

##

2017-08-01 09:46:54
Subhashree Sarkar
35978669
3.5
FOOD: It is good and affordable, the most famous dish being Chicken Ala Kiev. Priced reasonably at Rs. 200 only, it has two pieces of chicken coating filled with butter, served with mashed, boiled potatoes and yummy peas. The restaurant menu is quite varied and you can try out their other non-veg items like steak too.

DRINKS: This is what Olypub is famous for-drinks at a reasonable price. Though the menu mentions 30ml of some drinks, they only have 60ml minimum. The bar menu is the best, ranging from beer and whisky to rum and red wine-you will get all the brands you want, without making a hole in your pocket. We had 60ml of Old Monk, and GST is applied only on drinks.

AMBIENCE: Located in the "party para" of Kolkata-Park Street, it is one of the most pocket-friendly places to have a booze with your friends! The place is always brimming with youngsters hanging out with their friends and the sitting arrangement is pretty comfy, but could be a little more private.

STAFF: Staff is mostly good at their job, except that there is one waiter who keeps asking for a tips and a guard at the exit who does the same.

All in all, would love to go there again.

3. The ambience-  changed and renovated. Like it.. happy not to see the dust and smoke inside. it has turned livelier and happier. 

I was a regular in Oly and lost my faith in it with that incident. My visit this time had changed my mind. I congratulate and wish good luck to the management and hope this outlet remains one of the best attractions in Kolkata.

2017-07-06 00:11:23

7980651
3.5
Definitely a warm welcome by an Old Classic of Calcutta (this place was legendary before the name Kolkata sufficed) . The place where I would have ended up in college days to grab a snack and enjoy cheap alcohol.

The Steak is out of the world and has a classic Indian touch to it, the meat is juicy and succulent to the last bite served with a side of mashed potatoes and boiled peas with a sunny side up on the surface. Roast Chicken was pretty average with a basic taste. Alcohol is definitely cheap with an avg pint priced at INR 110 inclusive of taxes.

The let down is the ambience and the service quality, the ground floor is definitely a " No Go " it smells bad and looks like an old cranky pub from the 90's. The first floor seating is better and cleaner. The service though is equally bad on any floor and is a let down, be it cleaning the table or returning the change the staff is laid back and takes own sweet time to attend .

All in all the place to be just for gobbling Steak and enjoying a quick beer .

2017-04-25 22:38:20
Rupsa And Sagnik
16241875
1.5
Cheap booze .. Mouth watering food.. Cordial stuff and old Calcutta charm. After reading these in review after review with photos of mouth watering food both your heart and test buds feel tempted with desire to dive into that cozy , endearing heaven . You reach and push the door of this apparent ancient pub of calcutta, loadad with positive expectation as much as a double cheese pizza with extra cheese .. you enter and as soon as the dense fog of nostalgia lightens you see a place which looks like a smaller version of coffee house only with mirror on the wall and cushioned seats . You hear they have another level . You climb higher because you are culturally trained to always look UP for heavens .. but as you push the more fancy glass door and settle down, the bubble of nostalgia bursts and throws at you a waiter whose nosiness , unprofessionalism and ill manner can give tough competition to the coffee house staff, limited choice of alcohol brands and very oily food. Indeed in our age media has murdered reality . Oly pub taught us that in bitter way .

##

2017-03-01 21:13:59
Gaurav Dhar
6825941
4.5
This place will always hold a special place in my heart. It's not that I started drinking from there and also not that I have been visiting it for years but still there's something about Olypub that draws me towards itself. There may be many modern pubs opening in and around Calcutta but this will always remain special to me. So basically this is the cheapest place in Park Street to booze. I wouldn't recommend this place for a standard lunch or dinner fare but there are some gems hidden in that food menu which you can give a try. Some of them are the famous Beef Steak, Chicken A La Kiev and the Chicken A La Olypub. The waiters there have a strange attitude and won't answer your calls at once and you will have to tip them otherwise you will be met with very dirty looks but I guess that's a part of the charm of the Enigma called Olypub. This place is mostly crowded and If you take my recommendation it's worthy of the wait. Always try for the A/C section. And yes they accept only cash. As for me, I will keep on returning to this place till the day it exists.

2017-02-06 21:39:01
Pulak Dasgupta
30600093
3.0
On my recent visit to Kolkata, decided to give this place a try. This place was full at afternoon with college students and soon came to know reason behind it. Though located in Park Street area adjacent to The Park, booze provided here is quite cheap as compared to nearby famous places.

The ground floor have a normal seating area while the first one have AC, though both have dull ambiance. Staff is not friendly and you may have to wait for some duration before they come to attend you. That too behaviour lacks courteousness.

We asked for Tuborg strong which they said as unavailable. We then opted for Kingfisher strong and my cousin chose mixed grill which took around 20 minutes to be served. It consisted of potato wedges, saut√©ed veggies, chicken liver fry, bacon strips, mutton sausages with caramelised onion and a fried egg. I thought nothing can go wrong in a grill but the veggies and egg were cold.

Our next option was Miller's and this time I chose for their signature dish, Chicken Ala Kiev. This dish seriously fascinated me. Looks like a regular chicken cutlet but as you cut through, the goodness of butter will spread all over the place. It's served on a bed of mashed potatoes and with a portion of saut√©ed green peas. This dish is worth trying.

We ended up with 100 Piper's on the rocks and the final amount came less than 1k which is not at all bad. So definitely a place to hang out with your friend but don't have much expectations.

Price is reasonable.

##

2016-12-27 15:04:11
Mouli Bose
3033962
4.0
Started as Olympia Bar and Restaurant in 1947 and reborn as Oly Pub in 1981, is famous for its Chateau Briand.

I first heard of it from my dad, but of course he didn't take me there for obvious reasons. Every person who lived and studied in Kolkata will have fond (and embarrassing) memories of this place!¬†It's the place where most Calcuttans (like me) lose their pubescence virginity and try beef for the first time.
This is a place where you'll find a group of people start jamming out of nowhere, this is a place where you get to watch people getting drunk while getting drunk yourself, it is a place with the old Calcutta tag which I so love!

In the first year of college when we started going there it used to be a really dark, morbid place with torn, shabby upholstery and faded walls but of course we didn't care much; We were busy devouring the "forbidden" food. Those are the days when no one needed to provide ID to buy alcohol. But as months went by we became more choosy and stopped going there.

But. Like an year back I started hearing news of a renovated Only Pub, and tbh I was a bit startled with their new d√©cor. Even a few years back it used to remain mostly deserted on weekday afternoons, but since the relaunch it's almost always full with youngsters and loyalists alike.

Though something that hasn't changed a bit is the unfriendly waiters, but I don't really mind that. And trust me the food will soothe the frayed nerves. :3

üî∏ Chateau Briand (Beef Steak) : Their beef steak is one of the best in town. A juicy steak, caramelized onions, boiled peas, mashed potatoes with a mushroom on top. I don't know why, but I like their beef steak way more than

2016-10-22 17:05:42
Soham Ghosh
1833872
3.0
There was a time when Olypub used to be the best place to spend your evenings. The booze was cheap, the food was good and how many places actually served Chateaubriand? Sadly enough, those days are long gone.

The food hasn't turned awful thankfully. The steak is still edible and their ala Kiev still manages to pull in customers. They've actually improved in this segment, considering how bad the food was a year or so ago. I wouldn't recommend the food here at all, simply because it isn't even close to as good as some other places. But because Olypub boasts an amazing history and you're free to do most anything, does it actually have customers. 

The service is among the worst in Calcutta. They're slightly better than the Coffee House and that's saying plenty. The furniture is fine, and the crockery isn't terrible. For the price, I suppose you're treated to a decent lunch.

I wouldn't recommend Olypub to anyone, unless you're a beef fanatic. The problem with that is we expect people to ask us how we like our steaks. Olypub just skips that step and serves it to you. I've had one which was well done, one which was rare, and a couple other times when I could hear the cow moo. Steaks should be rare, but for pity's sake, ask your customers what they'd like. It's almost blasphemous.

Ambience/Interiors: 3/5
Service: 2/5
Food 3/5
Value for Money: 3.5/5

Ahhh, I am frankly a little confused about what to write about THE Olypub. Rather where do I start while writing on it. Do I start on one of those lazy afternoons when we used to visit there for a quick shot of Gin (so that the smell is not there) or a few years back, to one of those evenings where it was probably the only place in Park street where I could have relatively cheap booze with good food. For me, Olypub is the epitome of Park St or is it the other way round ? No, not the overpriced, upmarket cake joints, not those posh restaurants where you have to get in queue just to get in- Oly is one of those places where you feel at home. Its memories revisited.

I won‚Äôt waste time on how to reach and when to reach, because once you reach Park St, Oly is one place which can not be missed. Bang on one of the poshest roads in town, it boasts of a place where one simpleton can have a few booze with one of their many signature dishes and yet not feel murdered because of the price. Let‚Äôs come down to point now.

Just once you get in, hit for the first floor and please be ready to get disappointed because, if it‚Äôs evening time, the place is full. First floor is the place where all the sofas are there. There are 2 sections and I always always prefer the inside one more, for the sheer coziness factor. Settle in and start asking for the waiter. Like any good old fashioned joint, waiters here carry an air of attitude and are not too keen to service. But, after 3-4 regular visits, the attitude will change and the actual service will start. However, order for your booze (you‚Äôre not expecting any fancy cocktails here-right ??? ) and without wasting another moment, order for their Beef Steak. Please forget about the technicalities. Do you really care about whether its a perfect chateau briand cut or why they never asked you whether you want a rare-done or medium done ? Just enjoy the full done heap of meat (with the sunny side on top) that‚Äôll be dumped in front of you with few boiled vegetables and upon asking, the mustard bottle. With barbequed onions and mashed potato (they won‚Äôt serve you more), the sliced heap of beef meat heap is un-parallel.

Off course, while cutting through the slices and gobbling it with beer, you‚Äôll ask for the chicken liver fry. It‚Äôs again one of their specialties. Chicken liver, sauteed with chopped green chilly and onions in a an oily-semi-juicy manner is definitely recommended. Shamelessly, I order a buttered toast with it, simply to polish off the gravy from my plate.

Well, now that you‚Äôre kind of settled, look around. You‚Äôll find lots of your own selves around. At the next table, the kid, who‚Äôs constantly trying to be a hero in front of his girlfriend by gulping the small peg of vodka at one shot and choking at it and the lady looking around proudly ‚Äì isn‚Äôt that you some 15 yeas back ? See that table with the formally dressed middle aged gentleman (with mandatory tie off course) sitting with his lady colleague and enjoying some quality time, stolen from their mundane office life, isn‚Äôt this what you‚Äôre going to be in next 5 years ? Ohhh, by this time, you‚Äôve off course ordered for their chicken a la kiev and it has arrived, so come back to present time and dissect the thing. Just when you put in your knife, the liquid butter starts coming out and you‚Äôll start wiping it with the remaining piece of toast. See, toast is needed. They serve 2 pieces of a la kiev (god knows how at that price) and don‚Äôt mind sharing it with your partner. Experiencing foodgasm ? Go for your first round of smoke and come back. Earlier, they allowed smoking inside only, but like all good things in life, that‚Äôs prohibited now. For ladies, you may smoke in the back-alley in front of the ladies restroom, yes, you do have certain things waived off in life.

Come back and wait for the showstoppers. Yes, there are 2 of them and I guess you‚Äôve placed the order before leaving. The grilled fish and the cocktail sausage platter. Thankfully, they still serve Kolkata vetki. The portion size is getting smaller day-by-day, but who the hell cares. Its grilled to perfection and topped with some strange home-made sweet-tangy goddamn sauce, just to make the whole package more interesting. They serve some boiled vegetables (which I never had) and few pieces of fat, moist, homely finger chips- just the type your mom or wife prepares at home. The cocktail sausage, on the other hand, is a lone warrior. They just come around 8 pieces, without any accompaniments. The bottle of mustard will come handy now, pour some on the plate, roll the sausage in it and with closed eyes, put the whole damn thing in your mouth. Wash it down again with some beer (I guess, like any gentleman, you‚Äôve lost count of how many you‚Äôve consumed and drained out in the ground floor men‚Äôs restroom).

Ok, you can sit for how long you want in here, enjoy, chill. They prefer a laid-back service style here. Watch the young rebel beside you, watch him tear apart the current government over those pegs of Old Monk rum, and smile a little. Recognize him ? Didn‚Äôt you know somebody like him in your college days ?

While coming down, don‚Äôt forget to pack some of the chicken/ mutton patties from the ground floor counter. They make some off the best stuff at around 25/- per piece in town. I would rather suggest, to pacify your wife, pack some- they tend to vanish fast.

3.0
I rated it moderate as I personally like visiting this place and lot of fond memories are attached. Although a legendary outlet, but it may not seem very appealing to first goers and honestly it might actually not be. Some of the food here is excellent like the beef steak (absolutely delightful), the chicken ala kiev (outstanding) and the dry chilli chicken which has a special gingery punch to it. Other than that rest of the food is average at best. The liquor is neither cheap nor expensive, one who has been to most bars in the city would know it is moderately priced. There is nothing much of an ambiance, dimly lit sitting arrangement at the top with old sofas. It is comfortable and enjoyable in likeable company. But certainly a great place to relieve nostalgic moments. They dont let you smoke inside by the way.¬†
In short, if you wanna try out the beef steak and the chicken ala kiev, this is the place to be. If you wanna share a moment of the Kolkata culture you can visit this place. You may very well bump into some famous guy or the other as I have many times

Then ultimate den for booze at reasonably cheap rates in and around Park Street area. It has been there for decades maintaining it's brand value. This is more like Kolkata's very own Leopold cafe with its own distinct fame and charm. Recently we dropped in at Olypub during Durga pujo for a reunion with old friends. It was perfect. Maybe the ambience doesn't match upto that of new age pubs and cafes, but then Olypub wont remain the same if anything changes. Specially the delicious beaf steak, Chicken a La Olypub, a La Keif, etc. We went there in a group of 9 and we had beers sufficient enough to use the toilet twice or thrice. üòÇ The total bill came around 10k which was quite reasonable.

Overall, Olypub is there to stay as long as the spirit of Kolkata is alive in the people over here. Its legacy can't be defined by any ratings or reviews. But still if someone overlooks it's vintage charm and legacy, the food & booze deserves a 4 out of 5 and a 3.5 for ambience, staff & hospitality.

It's a low lit pub above and brightly lit ground floor.
The roof tells that its a pub of good ole days.
We ordered the following with soft drinks and the final bill was 905.

Chicken ala Kiev: two pieces served with mashed potatoes and boiled peas. The moment you cut molten salted butter flows out from the core. The crust is made of minced chicken with a piece of bone stabbed into to serve as a handle. It tastes wonderful. Good starter.

Mixed grilled platter: here it's served with chicken, mutton, beef and pork with mushrooms and poached egg. It had sausages, liver fries, salami etc. Overall very good in taste.

Chicken omelette: it's a regular big sized omelette topped with shreds of boiled chicken. Average in taste.

It's a lovely place to meet your meat cravings at a very economical price at a place like park Street. The dishes are fresh and great.

Oly Pub - One of the oldest pub of Park St.
=====
Intro + Location:

I don't think i need to introduce this pub. Oly pub is quite famous for it's beef steak and reasonably priced alcohol. Off late, there have been a lot of quirky cafes and pubs opening around which is making oly pub fade away in oblivion. It is divided into two sections. The upper section is a little dimly lit and way better than the ground floor one. On my last visit, the staffs were quite rude. This time when i went there, it was altogether better. Nevertheless, it was one of the Family friend's birthday so we went here for some drinks and steak.¬†

However, it is located in Park Street near Moulin Rouge or in the same line where Bar B Q and Kusum Rolls are situated.¬†
=====
What we ordered:

‚Ä¢ We ordered a couple of beers and whiskey. I am a whiskey person so i ordered one BP- Reserve collection. ‚úå‚úå

‚Ä¢ Roast Chicken Half - I had ordered this. It was served with fries, beans and boiled veges. It did not have poach egg unlike other servings. :| It tasted just alright. My friend's had ordered beef steak and mutton steak. The mutton steak had minced mutton.
=====
Pros:

‚Ä¢ Reasonable Alcohol
‚Ä¢ Good steaks
‚Ä¢ Good for group hang outs specially if the hang out is to get crazy
‚Ä¢ Service has improved since last visit few months back
‚Ä¢ Pocket friendly affair @ place like Park Street

Cons:

‚Ä¢ The roast chicken was not at all hot as expected.¬†
‚Ä¢ Not recommended to go on dates. :P¬†
=====
Meal for two: 500-1800 approximately (some may drink more :P) (including alcohol)
=====
Summary:

Food Quality 3/5
Food Presentation 3.3/5
Food Taste 3.1/5
Food Quantity 3.2/5
Hospitality 3.3/5
Ambiance 3.3/5
VFM 3/5
=====
Conclusion:

I personally found this place to be average. The ambiance,service, food, hospitality, etc etc. can be definitely taken to a next level. ¬†:)¬†
=====
Unbiased review based on my visiting experience.

2016-09-01 17:13:02
Shahrukh Ahmed
15540184
2.5
There are various reasons as to why a person visits a bar. Some visits to spend some time off, some to gulp in drinks which makes them be out of control and some just to accompany his friends. I am just the last category of person and a strict non-drinker of alcoholic drinks.
My first visit to this place was almost 6 months ago when two of my friends wanted to try some drinks out and wanted me to accompany them. Despite not liking it, I agreed to their whims and visiting Olypub.
The interior of this place was quite darkish being dimly lit. It had a two storey area and we got seated on the top one. Almost instantly, a person came for order and my friend ordered for themselves two hard drinks. I asked for a mineral water (literally).
The drinks arrived almost instantly and my water arrived a little later than 20 minutes. The whole time I sat there looking here and there and feeling obnoxious about the whole outcome. However, my friends were satisfied. They ordered for other drinks too which too came too fast and then again I reminded him of water which then arrived 5 minutes. After the hour long drinking session, we departed from the place.

Qs) Should you visit it?
Ans) People visit here for 'reasonably priced' alcohol. If you are in need to such things, pay them a visit.

Qs) Why have I rated them 2.5 stars?
Ans) People might argue that being a non drinker, I shouldn't have visited the place at the first place. However, I feel they should be liberal enough to serve each type of customers. I didn't like the way I was ogled at just because I didn't drink anything. Also, there were indirect pressure for tips at each points which is a big turn off. Taking all these factors, I felt it right to award them 2 and a half stars.

##

2016-09-01 12:15:10
Debolina Bhattacharjee
32147234
2.5
It is the place where many people tasted their beer for the first time. So it may be a nostalgic place for many people of kolkata. This was the place where I used to go back in 2013 or 14 for its cheap price of alcohol and chicken ala kiev (the most famous dish of olypub). If it was possible i would have rate 4.5 then. But the recent visits were not a good experience at all.
The first of its drawback is that they don't want to provide you an empty table (in case you are two) even if the crowd is small. They repeatedly tell us to share a four seater table with two other people. I mean you go to such a pub to relax and have drink. You cant share that with totally unknown people. Once we were made to wait for more than 20 mins for a two seater table when we could see many tables were empty and none of them were provided. We were so disgusted that we immediately left the place
Second the waiters have become very rude and will not listen to you even if you calk them ten times. They will come whenever they want and service has become too slow now a days.
Third even if you take glass and glass of alcohol you wont get complimentary snacks more than a single time. You have to repeatedly ask for it and then they will come up at the last moment.
Fourth the tables are not always cleaned and the washrooms are quite dirty and broken. A pub should always have a proper washroom.
Fifth is a very mandatory point that is starting from the waitor to gate keeper everyone asks for tips. Even if you don't see them at the time of entry you will definately see them asking for tips when getting out.
In spite of all these, the place still gather crowd because of the memories one had at their college life and the delicious dishes they serve. Even if you don't booze you can try this place just for the foods
Chicken a la kiev and chicken a la olypub are two of my favourite dishes. Mutton roast, mixed grill, beef steak, hamburger steak and cocktail sausages are few of must try dishes here. But don't try indian dishes. They never made it properly.

2016-08-13 18:34:30
Sreetama Chowdhury
20349784
3.5
Oly Pub is one of those age old pubs located in Park Street that has been doing business for over 50 years. Jam packed during any time of the day, Oly provides its customers with pocket friendly alcohol and some few classic dishes which resonate its British heritage. The pub undoubtedly keeps a very low range of alcohol, you would not get good cocktails or wine here, but if you are a college student with a couple of notes in your pocket and a hankering for some booze, Oly is the only deal. I have a personal liking for their beef steak and Chicken ala Oly. I wouldn't vouch for the cleanliness of the place or the magnitude of good service, the dirty glasses are sometimes very offputting. But multiple visits to this place has made it a den of nostalgia for several young and old Bengalis, for Oly has been the little den of new employment/ coming of age revelry for many.

This is one of the oldest bar cum restaurants located in Park Street,Kolkata.
This place is famous for beaf steak and reasonably priced alcohol.

Few days back I went there with my friends to try out their beef steak but it was not available.

Service:

This is something which they should really work on. The behaviour was good but they responded very slowly. I have asked for a spoon when I started having my food but they came up with it almost when I was done.

Overall:

Its a good old place in the heart of Kolkata to try out beef steak with alcohol.

##

2016-06-30 14:58:04
Varun Rajgarhia
31546427
3.5
LOCATION:

On the prime Park Street stretch right beside Moulin Rouge. Alternately, next to Kusum rolls on Park Street.

OVERVIEW & INTERIORS:

Dating back to the British Raj in India, this ¬†popular bar and pub has the old school to feel to it. If you want to know true Kolkata culture from the years gone by step right in and have a look at their menu. It will take you back to the golden era of Kolkata where everything was ¬†influenced by the erstwhile British empire. Interiors during my last visit which was ages back were ordinary. But I hear they have renovated the place and modernized it slightly. Nonetheless, its not the interiors you will seek when you visit the place.

WINE & DINE:

We called for Steak in Black Pepper Sauce, Crispy Fish Fingers and Chicken Reshmi Kebab. This was accompanied by a plethora of alcohol as we were old friends meeting after ages.

The thing which strikes out first about your experience is the amount of alcohol they serve per helping. Surely a small whiskey does not mean a 30ml standard peg here. It was more like 45 ml per small peg which would be great for people looking for cheap drinks on the otherwise expensive Park Street stretch.

The Fish Fingers were ordinary. They were not crispy but they were tasty. They did not serve Mayonaise ¬†and we had to make do with ketch up and mustard.¬†

The Chicken Kebab was also average. It was too dry as a reuslt of being overcooked.¬†

The Steak was little too hard. I feel that steaks should not be taken above Medium. A well done steak hides the quality of the meat used which I fear was the case here. Nonetheless, the suace itself was tasty and it was served with a single side fried egg, some mushroom and peas and a potato mash.¬†

Service was ok. The stewards have been here forever now so they have that typical cranky nature about them. But service is quick and the moto is to keep it simple. No fancy table mats or cutlery. Just good drinks and pub food which should not be analyzed much but should be enjoyed over drinks and good company.

FEEDBACK FOR IMPROVEMENT:

While I have been quite lenient with my review of the place as well as my score, I would be critical about the fact that cutlery and glasses need to be cleaned better. We had to actually use tissues to do the same on the table because we could see they had not been cleaned properly.

VERDICT:

Don't go there for ambience, food quality, sophisticated crowd, great service or great beverages. Yet this place is full. Thats because of the old world charm this place houses which cannot be replaced with either of the above mentioned points. Go there to feel a part of the Old Kolkata charm. You wont be disappointed.

##

2016-06-27 16:38:43
Souradeep
2003786
3.5
Popular for its beef stake, mix grill and cheap beer. Usually crowded by office gowers stopping here for there meetings. The ground floor is non ac and the 1st floor has dim lighting and has ac.
The beef stake is not that good as spoken about. The meat is stiff on the top layer and tender at the bottom. Although the taste is pretty good. Its served with mashed potatoes and boiled vegetables. Both of which lack seasoning and presentation.
A better option would be the mix grill which has chicken pieces, sausages, liver and bacon. Quantity wise its alright but not that filling. Bacon has a lot of fat and less meat. The liver served in the dish is soft but has a slight smell to it. Whereas the sausages are reall tasty.
Having your food with a sip of beer would surely make the food more tastier. Its worth going and trying out the place to have an experience.

But I hear they have renovated the place and modernized it slightly. Nonetheless, its not the interiors you will seek when you visit the place.

WINE & DINE:

We called for Steak in Black Pepper Sauce, Crispy Fish Fingers and Chicken Reshmi Kebab. This was accompanied by a plethora of alcohol as we were old friends meeting after ages.

The thing which strikes out first about your experience is the amount of alcohol they serve per helping. Surely a small whiskey does not mean a 30ml standard peg here. It was more like 45 ml per small peg which would be great for people looking for cheap drinks on the otherwise expensive Park Street stretch.

The Fish Fingers were ordinary. They were not crispy but they were tasty. They did not serve Mayonaise ¬†and we had to make do with ketch up and mustard.¬†

The Chicken Kebab was also average. It was too dry as a reuslt of being overcooked.¬†

The Steak was little too hard. I feel that steaks should not be taken above Medium. A well done steak hides the quality of the meat used which I fear was the case here. Nonetheless, the suace itself was tasty and it was served with a single side fried egg, some mushroom and peas and a potato mash.¬†

Service was ok. The stewards have been here forever now so they have that typical cranky nature about them. But service is quick and the moto is to keep it simple. No fancy table mats or cutlery. Just good drinks and pub food which should not be analyzed much but should be enjoyed over drinks and good company.

FEEDBACK FOR IMPROVEMENT:

While I have been quite lenient with my review of the place as well as my score, I would be critical about the fact that cutlery and glasses need to be cleaned better. We had to actually use tissues to do the same on the table because we could see they had not been cleaned properly.

VERDICT:

Don't go there for ambience, food quality, sophisticated crowd, great service or great beverages. Yet this place is full. Thats because of the old world charm this place houses which cannot be replaced with either of the above mentioned points. Go there to feel a part of the Old Kolkata charm. You wont be disappointed.

3.5
Popular for its beef stake, mix grill and cheap beer. Usually crowded by office gowers stopping here for there meetings. The ground floor is non ac and the 1st floor has dim lighting and has ac.
The beef stake is not that good as spoken about. The meat is stiff on the top layer and tender at the bottom. Although the taste is pretty good. Its served with mashed potatoes and boiled vegetables. Both of which lack seasoning and presentation.
A better option would be the mix grill which has chicken pieces, sausages, liver and bacon. Quantity wise its alright but not that filling. Bacon has a lot of fat and less meat. The liver served in the dish is soft but has a slight smell to it. Whereas the sausages are reall tasty.
Having your food with a sip of beer would surely make the food more tastier. Its worth going and trying out the place to have an experience.

Liquor price is cheap as compared OlyPub being in Park Street area and the liquor also being served fast after being ordered. Food price is also moderate. Behavior of staff remains the same, sometimes no reaction, sometimes being lazy and sometimes being rude. Overall same old place with same old environment but with new renovated and modified ambiance.

Situated amongst the string of restaurants in the popular Park Street area, this place is one of the most 'happening'(if I can call it that) hangouts for the youth and beyond for decades now. There are evenings where one has to stand in a huge queue for hours before getting a place to sit. So, if you want to go there and chill with friends over a plate of well cooked steak and few beers, then please go ahead. However if you are expecting amazing ambiance, authentic delicacies then this is not your place my friend.

Olypub, is a place which is irreplacable. It has been there for ages, and our previous generation talks of this place as lovingly as we do. Now that is no small achievement. The name itself brings a smile to the faces of most.

Now it has been revamped and the couches have been freshly upholstered. But most of my memories here were of worn out couches, stark white tube-lights and long queues at all times. The queue is still there, but the promise of ultra buttery a la kievs and saucy mixed grills make the wait worth it!

2016-05-21 14:54:14
Asit Saha
16333216
4.0
Olypub is not a restaurant, it is not a bar, it is not a night club - you just cannot categorise it. It is one of its kind. First and foremost, hardly anyone goes there for casual or fine dining, neither they flock there for only booze - then what is Olypub - it is an experience, dimly lit, tinkling of bottles and glasses, the waiters running to and fro, dingy spaces between tables made even more restricted by large groups flocking together - people ranging from intellectuals to pure alcoholics and the jewel in the crown being the impressive array of anglo indian khansama style food which these olypub goers will die for - chicken a la kiev, mixed grill, potato chips - a taste which no one can replicate - this is an experience unparallel and uncontested....

It is part of Kolkata's history ...Olypub is entrenched in the psyche of kolkatans...no amount of fine dining joints or restopubs can compete with this ....

I am deliberately not posting any photos here - let interested ones have their own first hand sensual pleasures

3.5
The story of most of us with Olypub begins right when we study for our XII Boards or may be in the beginning year of our undergrads, that is when we have just been introduced to drinking by our notorious group of friends. Olypub is one place which is considered to be safe heaven and no one here cares what the adjacent table does. This is probably why people would fret less even if it was the odd individual out smoking or drinking here.

The story of this place is usually the same for most of us. Take a chilled strong beer and a Beef Steak! That pretty much sums it all. The place is divided into two floors with the more sophisticated drinkers usually opting for the first floor while the hardcore ones, mostly coming alone preferring the ground floor. The waiters here are famed for their notorious and careless behavior not exhibiting even the slightest touch of professionalism.¬†

There was a time when I was a regular here and thereby I have had my fair share of experience. The drinks were decently priced, the food wasn't costly as well. The Steaks, Ala Kiev's, all of them used to be a perfect companion to the supercheap booze and neverending gossips with our friends. Not sure, how the place portrays itself these days, but I wouldn't have a clue about it any more as I have given up on drinking. But maybe, just once, I could pay a visit once again. If not for boozing, may be just for the sake of nostalgia!

Overcrowded, crammed, and noisy, you have to wait to get a table here. At the end of all the wait, you get very few items to choose from. This is where most Kolkatans lose their beef-virginity, and their teetotaler status, which is why Oly Pub holds a special place in the hearts of people here. It does have a sentimental value and an old-world charm, but that's probably all.

All in all,if we are a group of friends intending to catch up on some adda over cheap drinks and tasty food,oly it was,is and probably will be

Back to oly after almost a decade and boy was I in for a surprise. Now most of kolkata started their slippery slope here whilst in college . ##

2016-02-04 17:11:51
Kuntal
1390419
4.5
Food- 4/5.
Service- 3.5/5. ( Too crowded for service to be fast, don't order off the regular stuff, ask for quick delivery time of items)
Ambience- 3.5/5. ( A recent make over to 1st floor has uplifted the looks)
Price- 5/5.
Parking- 2/5 ( Considering right on Park Street).
Heritage- 5/5.
Value For Money- 4.5/5.

You walk in here, and you are very likely to brush your shoulder with some intellectual stalwart/ teen college guy with equal probability. This place is a conglomeration of every aspect of Kolkata. Its typically Bengali adda, place to vent out anger at bosses, place to cry over ex(s), place to romanticize, place to celebrate- one occasion and every occasion. Drinks very are dirt cheap. Signature dishes: Chicken A La Kiev (Buttery Russian delicacy ), Chicken A La Olypub ( an addition of bread toast and mashed potato gravy to Chicke A La Kiev), Prawn Cutlet, Fish Cutlet, Roast Chicken. Mutton cutlet is very nice too. There is a beef dish which I do not remember which I have heard is nice too. Drink- specialty here is rum with lime cordial and coke. Else try your own choice of drink- you get here dirt cheap. One strange thing, the waiter insist on tips, which you can give ( 10/20/30/40) depending on total bill amount as they don't charge service charges. The ambience is bit dark sorts, but given the history of being going here since past many years ( decade) can vouch for the good place to hang out with bunch of people. But yes its not a fancy place. So be aware of it. I personally make sure I visit just to soak in the spirit of the place at least once.

3.0
Its is one of the oldest and most popular bars in the city. You will come across many people who have not heard about Oly :D The booze is cheaper than many food is also moderate in cost. The quality of the place is on a decline over the years. They do not accept cards.

Food: They have a limited bar menu and due to huge sales, run out of certain drinks frequently. This place used to be famous for Steak, one of the earliest proponents of steaks in kolkata and they still cook a decent dish( must have one if you visit). Over all food is not that good though so beware of ordering anything extravagant.

Service: Service is lax, people are rude and opportunistic, you need to slip a few to he staff to get quick seats.¬†

Ambiance: very crowded and noisy place . You will frequently see drunk pople having quarrels and brawling with staff.¬†

Verdict: Visit for the steak and its popularity and to get stone drunk, not recommended for girls or dates.

2016-01-08 16:09:06
Ashish Gautam
1463992
3.5
This is a drinking den serving cheap booze in a not so pleasing ambiance but great food makes up for it. 

It is on the main road in park street and looks really promising from outside. But from inside its just simple seating in a room with bar. Still you have to wait for about 15-30 minutes to get a table in evening. Its always full and reason is its popularity among the people for its good food. Staff is also very average and is not like what you expect at a bar. But again cheap prices justify everything. 

I ordered their beef steak which took some time to arrive and was also not very good to look at as being served without any neat manner of serving with mashed potatoes, egg and boiled peas. But when it came to taste, it was a clear winner with its tender meat and brilliant texture fused with tongue pleasing taste. 

In all very much recommended if you want good food and cheap drinks without giving a damn to decor and ambiance.

1. Food: 4/5
2. Ambiance: 3/5
3. Service: 3.5/5
4. Value of Money: 3.75/5

##

2016-01-07 11:51:28
Abhijeet Singh
192945
4.5
It's a magical place, an old watering hole with charm and character. It's not the perfect place to be, you'll will find many a better bars and many a cheaper bars and many a bars with better ambiance and courteous servers, a place with more modern menu and fun drinks, but no place and I mean no place can be Olypub. Yes it's a bit rundown, but if you are out to have fun with friends isn't it better to be at a place with no fake attitude. If you feel the servers are don't care for you much its because they have a lot on their hands and if you want better service go somewhere else, you don't belong here. I am a regular and as some of the servers know me, so for me its descent, and say if you like the place but the service is the limiting factor for you, well would suggest you to do this, treat them well, be well mannered and slide in fifty bucks with your first pour, you won't have any complains after that. What we usually don't follow TIPS basically stand for To Insure Prompt Service, so go ahead and tip before you are served, the service won't disappoint you. I like the place as it has no ambiance, no mood setting music or interior decor; as a result it doesn't cater to a specific mood or a specific type of people. You'll find all sorts of people here, you can find a group of 3 to 6 college students sitting next to a middle aged man who is in for a quick drink before he heads home after a hectic day at work and right next to them you could find working professional, a group of old friends meeting after ages or say a bunch of party birds, boozing up before they hit the night clubs. This place has a certain quality cannot pinpoint, it has that special charm, to me it has a soul. There are better bars but none better for meeting fiends and just having a good time.

So even being a crowded pub altogether(with eventual loudness in the ambience), this place is an exceptional one which have its own legendary charm and deserves a 4+ rating.

##

2015-10-08 00:06:33
Sayantan Ghosh
3002940
4.5
If you are a Calcutta thoroughbred, then the name Olympia Pub , aka Olypub to us on Park Street will strum a few strings of your heart. I use the word Calcutta, not Kolkata because Olypub has its legacy ageing back to Calcutta days. The most iconic and one of the oldest bars in town (now partially renovated with modern decor) , most popular for its very very reasonable prices on drinks and the legendary Beef Steak. Back from my days in high school to present, its the most reasonable place to eat and drink in Calcutta . The taste of its food is also delicious , not to mention the best Beef Steak with soy Onions and Poach and the Chilli Prawns. This place even now, does not accept cards so please carry plenty of cash if ur going in for a heavy session. Cash is the only mode of payment there . A drink and bite will merely set you back Rs.300 there which is peanuts compares to prices nowadays...So have a try...cheers

##

2015-08-26 12:58:20
The Hungry Young Man
703164
3.5
'Olympus has fallen'.. the movie couldn't have been titled more aptly. Olympus Pub or more popularly Olypub is one such fallen angel from Kolkata. Once what used to be the most apt place for a social milieu, awesome food and dirt cheap booze, is now (and most recently) a refurbished, redone and modern rendition of the pub. The AC must have gotten efficient, but the service is still slow, the food overpriced and the portions small. Once can't really complain about the booze, as the government is to blame for the soaring prices :P¬†

Coming to the positives, I best like Olypub for the kind of crowd that it attracts and the conversations that flow across the floor. The booze is served and measured in a peg-measuring thingy right in front of you (unlike many a phony pubs). In terms of food, the beef steak (served rare, medium & well done) still stays a favourite and so does the complementary quarter plate of 'namkeen' (chanachur). Not to forget, the unexpected friend that you might end up making, after a few pegs of booze and a great conversation over a smoke.

happens to be one of the oldest pub in the locality with very reasonable pricing, a stand-up hangout for long relaxing session with friends. One speciality of this place apart from their food is drinks being poured right in front of you from respective bottles in proper peg measures.

2015-08-17 08:51:39
Abir Chaudhuri
15035411
4.5
The 2 things that come to a person's mind when he hears the words 'Oly Pub' are beef steak and drinks. If you don't spare much thought about the ambience, and just want to spend a great time with your friends having lip-snacking meals or drinking your way to glory, then this is the perfect place.  Though the top floor has been renovated, it still manages to grab a rating between 4-5/10. Though the top floor looks more like a pub, the ground floor still looks like  a coffee shop, only, without the coffee and with the alcohol. However, barring all that, the food is to die for here. For every connoisseur, the beef steak is always the first choice, so those who are going for the first time, do try it. Its quite the experience. The other options are chicken a-la-kiev and chicken a-la-oly pub. Both are great, but somewhat similar. I tried the mutton steak there, and I thought it to be a bit too crunchy and too sweet. Having drinks at Oly Pub is somewhat like a tradition in Kolkata. A genie in the bottle is that everything is surprisingly affordable, given that the restaurant's location is in the prime part of Park Street. I would suggest everyone who read this exceptionally long review to go there, not once, but as much as you can. Because it has always been a great experience

3.5
It is slightly difficult to fall in love with legendary Oly pub if one begins to go there at an advance age beyond one's student, college and early work life. It is like going to Maddox square at the age of 25 for the first time.

Oly Pub mostly rates high on nostalgia and associated memory of youthful friendship and good times. If you have neither ( like me), you are left with pretty average food, cheap booze and a dingy place with bad washrooms. Of course the beef steak is good, but often the blunt steak knives make u wonder if u should have carried your own cutlery set.

So basically if you are like me, then go to Oly Pub with a friend who loves Oly Pub and has grown up there and go with a pretty low expectation threshold as well. It can be quite a let down otherwise in the company of others who are as new as you.

Well here's my experience which I had at this place when I visited once again after a long time. This arguably is the cheapest pub on Park Street, I say this with a popular vote.

The ala kiev, which looked dwarf to what they used to serve, almost arrived before the beer and its trademark snack. Then came the plates minus tissue papers but thankfully with fork and knife. Yes, the quality of the food and the service has deteriorated but who cares when all you care about is your drink.

The same old brands and in same old glasses, bring back a lot of college days memories. The place has not grown up a day. Not to mention the eccentricity of the waiters and their usual denial of your existence after you've ordered your drink.

But still the relentless chatter, the restlessness of the waiters and the taste of the beer after a hard day's work, these are all you can experience when you visit olypub. Cheers mate...

The prices have gone up significantly since when I first went to this place, but they still remain within reach for college students. The place is best for beer( though I sometimes order vodka or whisky-soda) and it keeps a limited selection of every spirit, though it appears otherwise on the menu. Food is so-so and the so-called legendary Beef Steak is oily and overcooked. The Chicken a la Kiev is delicious though and the mixed grill platter is alright. On Saturdays and Sundays though, one has to wait a long time before getting a seat and unless you get a seat upstairs, the seating is dim, crowded and noisy.

Olypub has always been a symbol of the Old Calcutta charm. This legendary pub which once defined Bangali Adda over beer and steak has been gradually deteriorating in quality and service over the years. Olypub was once a place we HAD to go once a week for the cheaply priced booze and the lip-smacking food. Good Old Days! 

I visited Olypub the first time after they renovated and modernised the place. The interiors are now amazing! The decor is nice but the service still lousy. Tried my usual favourites - Cocktail Sausages, Chicken A la Olypub and Chicken A la Kiev and had a couple of Beers to wash it down with. I found the quality of the food surprisingly much better than my last visit - But still not as delicious it used to be once upon a time & the quantity isn't as good as it used to be either. 

Olypub, in my verdict is still the most popular watering hole in the city and is a Must Try for anyone looking for fairly priced alcohol and good food. But for regulars or others who have witnessed the old charm of Olypub, it's still not upto the mark.

##

2015-05-31 12:19:35
Ranbir Sen
3018248
3.0
Olypub has been and continues to be an iconic venue on Park Street where reasonably priced alcohol and the celebrated 'Chateubriand Steak' (which is a steak cooked with a thick cut from the tenderloin) appear to be the reason for the high demand. The quality of food has dropped considerably over the years, however it is still difficult to get a table without waiting. Although there has been a total makeover with respect to the interiors, the service is incompetent and bearers appear to be constantly attempting to hurry the order to enable the table to get vacated for the next waiting customer. Due to the high demand for the Chateaubrian Steak, these are churned out in large numbers from the kitchen resulting in a situation where at most times the meat remains uncooked to a certain extent. The bearers no longer ask if you would like it rare, medium or well done and  it is usually served very well done which makes it difficult to cut and eat. My recent visit with a group of friends wih whom we have been visiting for more than fifteen years, was a disappointment, but the saving grace was the nostalgia and memory associated with this place. A few dishes like the fried chicken liver are worth a mention and the mutton cutlet is best not ordered. Overall, whilst Olypub will always remain a favourite with most people because of the emotional connect and pricing, one may need to choose other places due to the aspects of quality and service.

2015-05-21 19:20:42
Sourajit Karmakar
1190958
3.5
Good hangout place for young people and cheapest booze at park street!

 If you want to have lots of booze and have fun with your friends group then this is the best place at park street. Olypub is a place where mainly young people come so ambience is rowdy, not for family visits. The 1st floor has been recently redecorated, now it looks pretty good! Waiters are fast but sometimes a little arrogant.

This is one of those places where you can drink a lot without having to worry about the price. Best place to drink beer. The beer and beef stake combination is still kick ass. Their mutton ham steak, chicken ala kiev are also great. Although over the years size has reduced and prices gone up, they still are as tasty as ever. However if you are making dinner plans then better avoid this place. Here mostly you get good snacks items which are good with drinks. Main course items are there but they are not that great and priced little high. Chili chicken has too much onion, kebabs are average, roti costs too much, chicken butter masala is average too. In short olypub is great for boozing and having fun, not good for dinner. If you have dinner plans then after boozing here go to golden dragon.

2015-03-19 12:38:05
Jaysurya Deb
13928581
4.0
I am not giving a 4-rating for the ambiance or for the decor or for the quality of food - but for the sheer experience.

This is one of the oldest watering holes in the city and is rightly located on the street which speaks volumes of the influence that English culture has on Calcuttans!¬†Anyway, this place has two floors - the ground floor is non-ac section where people can smoke without much fuss and the first floor is the air-conditioned one where people would need to step out into a corridor at the back to smoke.

The ambiance is that of a college canteen, only cleaner. The furniture and fixtures cannot be more simple. The service is prompt and the waiters usually know the menu like the back of their hand. The pricing is very economical for the entire menu including alcohol - which is why the place has never got out of style, one might say.

If you're planning to visit on a Fri-Sat evening, please ensure you're there early - I myself don't know what 'early' means for this place since I have tried to enter at various hours but have almost always had to wait in a long queue. The place is usually thronged by mid-senior to senior intellectual folks who gather together to relive those college times; also visited, in equal numbers, by youngsters who like being associated with this tradition.

The place is brightly lit with tube-lights and is usually noisy - hence, warm, romantic evenings can't be planned here. However, people who wish to check out the culture in Kolkata,

2015-03-01 23:30:39
Ujwal Choudhary
1054168
3.5
Location: A stone's throw from Kwality Restaurant (towards McDonald's). 

This place has always been among the few chill out places I resort to. I don't know how I missed on reviewing it. Olypub is a Ground+Mezzanine type pub serving liquor at low prices along with delicious non-vegetarian and not so delicious vegetarian fare.
Earlier this place had a non-descript ambiance with tattered carpets but, now post-renovation, the ambiance has been improved to be a classic style place. Having a mix-match lighting of modern as well as antique wall-mounted lights with photo frames across the walls and wooden flooring on the mezzanine makes it a great place to unwind. 
The ambiance at the ground floor however, remains nearly the same.

Have always been here to unwind along with friends over alcohol, accompaniments and at max a plate of potato wedges or onion fritters (for myself). 
- Low priced liquor.
- Great accompaniment.
- Oily and saltless potato wedges, always.
- Tasteless fritters.

‚Ä¢ Have been here with non-vegetarian eating people who have marked the Chicken A La Kiev & Chicken Cutlet from their kitchen as a thumbs up. :)

‚Ä¢ A negative for this place is, even after the menu being widespread (only non-vegetarian, the vegetarian feels quite limited), most of the items aren't available at all times.
Plus, a few that's available, lack finesse.

The staff here has always been a bit grumpy and not so friendly. But, this doesn't hamper their service speed much, always at a standard speed.
Prices do not seem to pinch the wallet (with respect to liquor and non-vegetarian fare). Might be a pinch (with respect to the vegetarian fare).

Overall has always been a good experience.
- Wish the staff was a bit friendlier and less grumpy. :)
- About the remaining vegetarian fare, would update soon. :)
- The goodwill wouldn't take you a long way if ways aren't mended soon.

Would have given this place a four star rating, but, minus 0.5 due to the disappointing vegetarian fare.

2015-02-26 21:24:42
Tirthadeep Das
6513121
4.5
Legend- wait for it - dary!
Oly Pub is an institution in Kolkata, and one of my favorite places to eat. If ever I'm in need of an eatery, and can't decide where to go, Oly Pub is THE place that comes to mind. It's like your favorite blankie.
I've been to Oly before and after they renovated the top floors and I like it. Downstairs they still have the Pub like feel with the bar and plastic chairs and table arrangement. It's one of the few places in Kolkata with that Pub ambiance. And it certainly sounds like one. But you can still have a good conversation with friends. The upstairs, after the renovations, has become the fine dining part of Oly, a place where you can sit and have a regal dinner with friends and family. With dim lighting, proper sofas and tables, the upstairs and downstairs are two completely different atmospheres. With this improvement, it's possible to get children and family to eat out at Oly, cause people should.Have whatever opinions you want about the ambiance, the food is undeniably amazing. Call me monotonous, but whenever I go to Oly, I have to order the beef steak. It is amazing. Another positive of Oly is the alcohol. Cheap and authentic. Oly is very well priced and it more a budget eatery than anything else.Not much needs to be said about Oly Pub, apart from Legend - wait for it - dary!

2015-02-23 23:53:38
Kaustav Sen
1088586
2.5
Come to kolkata, go to Park St, and ask any guy, where do u get the cheapest booze and good beef steak, they ll point you out towards this place. Even zomato says that! Based on this legendary reputation, three of us went in. The menu card looks promising, but mind the words, LOOKS, but isnt. Thats because a lot of things are missing. Nothing else other than scrambled eggs was available in the egg catagory.¬†
Anyway, Beef Steak, Pork Sausages, Scrambled Eggs and a Prawn Cutlet was ordered. Plus, we had beer. Pint, they dont have. Out of the whole list of beer, they have just 3 variety. Anyway moving on...Beef Steak, juicy, and well done. Worth the money. Pork sausages, small ones, serve about 8 pieces of them, slightly salt heavy, but is nice. Scrambled eggs, standard issue stuff, nothing wrong with it.
Then, tragedy stuck us. The prawn cutlet arrived. Two of them...they appeared nice. And before i began, i pulled out the tail, and we laughed that we have been tricked, and that there was no prawn within. First bite, what the hell is this thing. There was no taste of prawn in any way, the thing tasted only of onions and had a bit of prawn flavour. We managed to finish only one. We ordered fish fingers and a mixed grill. Fish finger was again, so so, and tasted okay with the mustard, while the mixed grill could have been better. And there were bones in the meat pieces, didnt enjoy it much.
The waiters need to be more polite and be a bit more attentive. Also, they demand a tip, which immediately caused us to withdraw the little amount we were planing to leave.
To end, I ll say, this place is running only on the reputation, and most definitely not on the food quality, and it isnt so cheap after all, if u factor in the availability of the cheaper stuffs.

##

2015-01-17 19:21:49
Rohit Chatterjee
414951
4.0
One of those essences which make Park Street what it is. I have been to Olypub just a handful of times, but all those times have been quite memorable. The place remains pretty crowded on all days, but getting a table isn't usually a problem, unless it's a special occasion (you should take a look at the queue outside on Christmas day). It has a very old-world feel about it, and the bare minimum interior design adds to that. 

Olypub is a great place to hang out with your friends over a few rounds of drinks. The liquor is available at decent rates, and once seated, the conversation just flows. As for the food, I have had either the chicken a la Kiev or the beef steak whenever I have been here, and both the items are worth a try. The former is actually considered one of their specialities. 

Olypub lacks the zing of many of the modern pubs, but this is the place where memories are made. If you aren't a teetotaller, this place should definitely be on your to-visit list.

Olypub spells nostalgia. My first pub experience. In those days i was a non-drinker. Upon entering, the strong smell of liquor was enough to make me dizzy. I spent my entire time covering up my nose. Such idiotness! And now, for me, olypub is the place to be. I learnt to drink, sitting here in olypub. Be it a birthday celebration or catching up with friends or passing time or celebrating the onset of Durga Pujas, olypub is where we head to. Where else will you get a small vodka peg for 50rs? Olypub has stood by me in times of broke or otherwise. I have never seen an empty olypub except one instance when i visited it around 11am. But even then it had cusromers. Even the stench of liquor from the water bottles instigate a feeling of nostalgia. The food is good as well. The french fries had the exact amount of crispiness, the chicken ala kiev has the exact amount of molten butter in it, the legendary beef steak is perfectly cooked and so on. My only complaint is, i always find the sauteed veggies with the steaks to be stale. Price is really reasonable. Have spent hours here, so much so that sometimes the waiters have to shoo us out because its 15minutes past their closing time. Please don't go there if you prefer a fine drinking experience. Totally no-no for the so-called-elite showoffs. But remember, olypub is a class of its own. Simply apart from any other pubs that charge you 4 times the rate of olypub. A perfect hangout for students and office goers alike. Best place to be with friends or foes. Highly recommended. Cheerie!

Kolkata today thanks to its century old food loving and preserving culture, has mushroomed numerous restaurants, bars, food parlours to experiment with new and unique food items. Give it a try.

##

2014-10-31 20:48:19
Arnab Deb
237977
4.0
I have been to this place a couple of times whenever been to Kolkata and it has always been a bit of fun for me.

Being from Bangalore, this is the first time I have experienced a place like this which more than a Pub kind of feels like a Shady Bar but actually it isn't. The crowd which comes here looks quite decent and they stay well mannered. Even there is a good amount of female crowd who come there and are quite relaxed because the overall crowd is good.

I like the old feel of it using the basic wooden chairs and tables. The big steel "Almonard" type of stand Fans, the old liquor bottles they use to serve you chilled water. The first time when I saw waiters serving the ice from a steel bucket using those big steel spoon like thing which I guess is called "Hatha" in Bengali and is used to serve rice, I was like "What the Hell is this" and i couldn't control my laughter. It just took me back to our community Durga Puja celebrations where we used to get served with Rice and Khichdi like this from the bucket.

Anyways, coming back from Memory Lane to this place, the USP of this place is the liquor price. After drinking in couple of places in Bangalore, this place feels like a paradise and I tend to drink more here thinking that " I don't know when will be the next time I can be here again". 

The food also is value for money and quite good, I tried the Chilly Chicken which was decent. Also after reading couple of other Zomato user reviews, I tried the Chicken Ala Kiev (which I strongly recommend as something new to try), and i really liked it especially the look of the dish and the way hot melted butter was oozing out of it when I had the first bite. Mmmm.. Drooling now?? Probably the next time I go there, will try the Chicken A la OlyPub (Can't have the Beef Steak).

Now coming to waiters. They always seem busy and if you give them some order while they are passing by, they just make an irritated face and show their raised hand and ask us to wait. But they do get your order without much delay. Though I felt this was funny (Not funny for the regulars I guess) but probably if they could just improve on this along with the cleanliness and some other minor things of this place, it will be even better (then I would have given 4.5-5 may be) but I guess you can't expect waiters with good attitude when you are paying so less (I was really not expecting Air Conditioning at this price + there is no additional taxes on your final bill which in Bangalore easily increases the bill by 20-30% on top of really expensive liquor and food prices),  but at least for me, even this attitude of theirs somehow adds to the fun element of this place along with the others I mentioned above which makes me wanna go there every-time I visit Kolkata,  as all this is quite new for me.

Anyways, I would say it's a great place to hangout with your buddies. You can just keep ordering your drinks and some decent quality food without worrying that it will dig a deep hole in your pocket. For first timers, I guess they will really like this new kind of experience especially people like me who are new to this really different Kolkata culture.

When one speak of cheap booze in the hottest zone of the city, only one name will come to mind - Olypub. 2014-10-08 23:21:40
Hrishikesh Kar
1050962
3.5
Prime location, cheap booze, nice crowd(read hot girls & occasional celebrity presence), moderate food, memories of bygone era- put all of them together & they will spell only one thing- popular youth destination & there is a pub in the town that checks all the above boxes -OLY PUB. Located at one of the most precious location of kolkata (park-street near the park hotel) this pub stands there from the time I can recall. As the name suggests this joint is actually a pub in all the given sense though some vital features are missing of a pub in here still it can be proudly presented as an old school pub means all the regulars know each other & so do the waiters. I can't possibly add much to what is already been written or said about this place so I will try & keep it short. The entire establishment is divided in two floors. The ground floor is more specious where as the first floor is more private, well nothing is really private here, on a busy weekend you may will have to share your table with a stranger (note- if you are lucky you may get a beautiful company & sometime even a celebrated company.) Now coming to the drinks, the menu says that they regal an array of drinks where in reality only a limited types of drinks are available. There is a bad news for all my ‚Äúsmoker‚Äù brothers & sisters as well. The age old ‚ÄúFag balcony‚Äù is been transformed to ladies ‚Äúrefreshment‚Äù room recently so if you crave a fag during your drinks you need to go all the way out of the main door & puff some fresh air along-with. Well if I say that half of the ‚Äúbangalies‚Äù would have never tried beef (no offense meant to any community) if there was no oly or their famous beef-steak, I wont be exaggerating at all. My friends who have tried it says that the quality of it deteriorated significantly but I cant really shed any light on that. Overall the quality of the food is moderate. The menu is a mix of European classics & Indian traditional foods. For me the main problem with their food is their inconsistent quality & the time it takes to get out of the kitchen & get served in front of you (it often gets cold). The service of the waiters is so so, unless you are a regular. If you are planning to visit it on a weekend you should better be there by 5 in the evening or rather prepare yourself for a long & I mean a really long wait. & don't get fooled by the tag ‚Äúcheap booze‚Äù, it's not cheap by any means but it definitely is cheaper in comparison to the other pubs around..

##

2014-09-29 20:16:31
Apoorv Raj
996557
1.0
So I had been hearing about this place since I had set up camp in Kharagpur. In spite of having visited Kolkata many times during my 4 years at Kharagpur, I never got around to visit Oly, as it is fondly called by the student community at my college. Now that I started living in Kolkata, I just HAD to visit this place.

To our utter disappointment, this place and its food: just not worth it. You get better food at small scale restaurants in Kolkata. And they should call themselves "Oily Pub" for the quantity and quality of oil they put in their food. I have a thing for restaurants who open up without having everything on their menu, and it's not good. We asked for chicken tandoori, to which the waiter replied that none of the tandoori items were available. We ordered  beef steak and roasted chicken.

The roast chicken was served with a slimy looking sauce, some random *boiled* vegetables, and some fried potato fingers. The potato was smelling as if it was made yesterday and kept in the open. The chicken was OK, but the sauce applied on it was horrible. I had to try to wipe it off and have just the chicken. The sauce left a bitter taste which was unbearable. On complaining, they said that's the way their "master sauce" tastes. God save other dishes in which they use their "master sauce".

The  beef steak was equally, if not more, horrible. Served with boiled peas, mashed potatoes and egg. The meat was rubbery and tasteless. Let alone cutting, it was difficult even to chew. Even the sweet lime soda was so sweet it could make you vomit.

Plus the place is so ugly and shabby. Waiters are ill-mannered. After having such emetic food, giving a tip was out of the question. After we took back the change, the guy stood there, asking for tip. We calmly refused saying we didn't like the food at all. To our surprise (not so much), he arrogantly said "khana jaisa bhi tha, service toh theek tha na" (I don't care how the food was, but the service was OK). Then he went back taunting us aloud "Khana nahi pasand aya inko" (they didn't like the food). Well, duh. While leaving, the gatekeeper also asked for tip.

In short, I want my money back from every person who made such a big deal of this place and the beef steak. Go only if you want drinks with your friends which will not burn a hole in your pocket.

To summarize it:

Food: Horrible

Ambience: Murky

Service: Well, no adjectives

Avoid it at all costs. There are a hundred, if not a thousand, places better than Olypub in Kolkata, which will cater to your expectations and budget.

2014-09-12 07:12:41

3.0
In a middle class Bengali famliy where the idea of  having "beef" is almost considered a sacrilege, OLYPUB has always acted as a safe haven for tasting the "prohibited food." I had my first taste of beef at Olypub only, in my college days and thousands of college students have their first venture with beef here itself, for a long long time. And when you are doing something surreptitiously, the fun increases manifold. I have many fond memories with this place.



The colonial charm, the beef steak, chicken a-la kiev - all these have turned Olypub into a folklore, add to that the much cheaper price of the alcohol served over here. To walk down the memory lane and to revisit my college days, I went there a few months back, after a long gap of few years. The setup didn't seem to have changed much, neither the ambiance or the uniform of the staffs. With great expectations, I ordered for Beef Steak. Unfortunately, it was stiff and chewy and while I was trying to cut it, the whole table was shaking, so hard it was ! I looked around and realized that it was not my only table that was shaking, but all the tables who ordered for beef steak. I thought probably it was a bad day. So, I went there again in the next few days. It was even worse, the tables were shaking even more violently... I left hope and somehow managed to gulp it down with beer. I was disappointed. I could hardly match the same beef steak which we enjoyed thouroughly in our college days. Probably, things were not so easy to get then as they are now. The old charm of Olypub was gone (at least to me) and I am not too sure whether it should revive any more. So, I feel its best to live with my college days nostalgia instead of tarnishing the happy memories that I have with this place.

2014-08-27 23:21:05
Boudhayan Ghosh
1312809
4.5
OLYPUB

The name smells of Beef Steak n Chicken Alakiev.
The food:

1. Beef Steak was awesome. Though the peas and mashed potatoes could have tasted better. The beef... was awesome. Super softtt n tenderr.

2. Chkn Alakiev- As ur knife drills into the piece of poultry, liquid butter shall fill up ur plate. Ample use of butter makes this continental dish perfect.

Score for food- 4/5.

The Ambience:
You may call it cheap n down market... shabby tables, chairs, old n worn out cutleries, but we call it typical of Olypub. We are regular at plush upscale restaurants. We love this change.
Score- 3/5.

Value for score-
The most awesome part. Four pegs of top notch whisky, two plate Beef Stake, two Chicken Alakiev. (One plate would have impressively served two persons). Pocket pinch- Rs 1500/-. Authentic drink, authentic food, good time.

Overall score- 4.5/5.
