2014-08-20 11:30:19
Abhishek Pal
2797818
2.5
'Pub' in Calcutta....literally refers to this famous pub named Olypub.I mean almost everybody has been to this place,at least once in their entire lifetime.
Considering the typical Gypsy/ Hippie culture of Kolkata,this place provides you the best(of liquor and entertainment).
The entertainment over here is of course of a different level.You visit Olypub and you will hear this constant chitter-chatter that surrounds you(much like the noisy pubs on London).
The smoking zone is on the ground floor and the comfort zone is on the first.
Friends provide the best company to you in places like this.Hop in to Olypub after a tiresome Photowalk or simply on a weekend with your friends for relaxation,or with your Old School mates whom you meet after ages.
This place has got the antique smell of decoration and of course of the liquor it serves(they also serve Chivas 16 years).
The pub is also famous for the beef steak it serves,happens to be the best in Kolkata.
If you're a music lover hop into this place early afternoon,have a few pegs,enjoy yourself and strum the guitar a little to get everybody into the jig.
Famous personalities like Anjan Dutt and other eminent musicians-everybody has been and spent a portion of their valuable commercial time at Olypub.
One can try the Chinese dishes here,but the Chilli Chicken they provided last time was so Chilly that I literally gave it up half way.
Also the pub authorities should start serving liquor like the Smirnoff Mango Vodka and the Bacardi White Rum Green Apple Flavour,and the also various fruit juices.
The last time I visited this place,I found a cat in one of the vents.
All in all Olypub is till date the most renowned pub of Kolkata,but it is now time for the Management to go for a makeover of this place,and also take a step towards regulating the price of the liquor served here.

2014-08-17 22:38:33
Sayan Ganguly
3183185
5.0
Where do I even start when reviewing Olypub? The place brings back so many memories from my decade long tryst with it. It would not be possible for me to review this place objectively as it would be difficult to separate the tangibles (food, quality of service, etc.) from the intangibles (ambience, associations with the place, quality of crowd, etc.). I had my first peg of alcohol in this place. We were in the final year of school when we started visiting this joint. Back then, it was a smoke filled room (smoking inside the premises wasn‚Äôt banned then) where one would occasionally find rats scurrying around and waiters appeared more inebriated than we were by the end of our sessions. Although we started visiting Olypub primarily because the booze was cheap, the place gradually grew on us. It was a place where you can grab a beer with a group of friends and talk incessantly on everything under the sun from Kafka to Kinks to Kubrick! For those of us who are in our mid/late twenties, Olypub to us was the equivalent to what coffee house was to our predecessors. On somber Saturday evenings we, a group of ten, could easily be located at a table in Olypub. Also, the food was absolutely ecstatic ‚Äì from the amazingly sumptuous beef stake to the opulent Chicken ala olypub and the lip smacking cocktail sausages; made us come back for more. 

Slowly our group disbanded. I left Kolkata for good; and only came back a month before after six years of drifting places. So visiting Olypub after a long time was again a great experience. The ground floor was made air conditioned. The scurrying rats have disappeared now, and new faces have acquired the tables. The waiters have also become more courteous and I did not see the old ‚Äòchacha‚Äô who once suggested me that I should drink more, as even his younger son drinks much more than that ! The food was to die for‚Ä¶once again! Although the beef stake was quite smaller than what it used to be back then. All in all, the pub was still the same; and it‚Äôs for the best that some places do not change with time.

Beef steak, cocktail sausages, Chicken ala Kiev, Cheap Booze. CHECK. That for me sums up Olypub. At first the place might not look really appealing, but it would eventually settle in because Oly serves some real good food. The atmosphere inside if pretty chilled out, the service is real quick and the staff, a little intimidating. Unlike its name, this place is not just a pub, but definitely serves mouth watering food. ##

2014-06-23 21:45:35
Kanchan Yadav
777965
4.0
This place, which used to be mostly empty on weekdays even just a couple of years ago, is a famous hangout for youngsters these days. Oly is mostly famous for its beef steak. Though the mixed grill is also quite talked about, I didn't like it that much due to the presence of bone in chicken pieces.
Now, the thing about their beef steaks, on our earlier visits, one beef steak used to fill a person completely and more. But due to the reduction in size on our last visit we actually ate, to our surprise, two beef steaks each. But even though the size was reduced, it still tasted just as good. On some days though, some unfortunate person may get a very undercooked slice of beef, which had happened to me before, and to avoid that you should mention that you want your steak well done. 
The Indian tandoori, curries, and fish fingers are also quite well, as is the fresh lime soda. Also due to the relative cheapness of prices, not that much of a pocket pinch. However on some days they make a hassle with underage kids ordering beers, demanding an identity card. 
There are a few downsides of the place though. First is the waiters. They are very unprofessional, and non courteous. You have to ask them repeatedly to clean your table, or to serve your drinks. And eating on a table cluttered with dirty dishes is not a very pleasant experience. Also, you have to opt for a dine in here. Their parcel system is really, really bad. The one time I tried to opt for a take out, all three packages opened in the middle of the road and started dripping ferociously. 
Third, due to the over publicity of the place these days, a bunch of unpleasant crowd is often seen. In a pub in the heart of park street, it is uncomfortable if teenagers (and not teenagers, in some cases) get drunk and leer at you all the way from their own  table.
Though I bantered a lot about  the downsides, I know I'll keep going to that place again and again.

##

2014-06-16 11:08:50
Ruchismita Mukherjee
444517
3.5
What's unique about Calcutta is an almost Daliesque persistence of memory: a longing for things past, a prepeonderence of all things sepia and a permamnent colonial hangover - even as innovation, globalisation, and consumerism grips the city slowly, something's about Calcutta remain exactly the same.

One such monolith, is an ancient watery hole, a grimy, bustling, messy, smelly but oddly beautiful and atmospheric speak easy located at the heart of Calcutta's night-out paradise: Olypub or 'Olympia' as it originally used to be known. 

Try the mildly mangled, colonial fare - the superbly popular beef steak, the hamburger steak, the mixed grill, the bizarre chicken ala keiv and the drenched-in-oil finger chips; Let the drinks flow, the usual spirits poured in generous pegs into grimy glasses downed in massive volumes by the junta, keen for a respite from the work-life, talking, shouting, screaming, singing, loving, laughing, crying and at times, puking their hearts out.

Olypub is an idea, a jaded, tired, care-worn idea of being and arrival, of mirth and revelry, of exotic satiety and forbidden romance, an idea that's way past its prime, an idea standing on long uncared for legs, but an idea that's lit everyday by the needs and wants, the moods and dreams of the many who still feel a sliver of peace and happiness from their lives within the shadowy confines of this ancient abode of a lost city, echoing a forgotten time and a phantom, yesteryear charm.

2014-06-16 08:11:37
Vicks

The only restaurant in park street which has utterly disappointed me especially because so many people had recommended this place to me and also my faith in zomato got breached! Visit this place only if you wanna booze with friends,and don't order any food from here,that would be my earnest request to all the foodies!

Recently visited Oly Pub after a long time. It was late college days when we used to come here. But I was utterly disappointed this time. Don't know whether my taste changed or it was because of the same un- improved, shoddy ambience of the place.
I went there with 7 of my friends. There were 3 ladies in our group. That's why we chose oly pub. One big advantage with this place is you can always go with your girlfriend or colleagues as you can find numerous girls here.
As we entered, we found the place to be  immensely crowded. A waiter greeted us with utter rudeness just to make his own way from first floor to ground floor. We found the gents toilet to be clean, but the ladies toilet very much soiled.
The status of the crowd on the ground floor was not upto the mark. On the first floor, it was ok.
Now the drink and food. Waiter came to us after quite a while, we ordered 4 Smirnoff, 1 kingfisher blue and one breezer, lime cordial and sprite.  With utter surprise, they didn't give separate glasses, poured alcohols in the same empty water glasses, which were just the old shabby ones and not that clean too. Now, no sign of sprite and ice cube. Aftet a good 10 minutes when we started to make some noise, the waiter banged a whole bucket, full of ice cubes and sprite on the table. I was really annoyed.
Now we ordered dry chilli chicken, butter and plain nan and chicken butter masalla.
Dry chilli chicken was punchy in taste, but it was cooked in street-style and was Not looking or smelling premium. Nans were okies. But, the disaster was the chicken butter masalla. It was very bland in taste and was very casually cooked. Bill came around 2200. Ok... But china town gives a much better ambience, food quality and better service. After that day, will never visit there again.

##

2014-04-12 01:10:44
Aninda De
499094
3.5
To be true Olypub is not an ordinary joint. Its not just a simple watering hole where you can get alcohol cheap & spend a few hours sozzled away. Olypub seems to be a cultural turnstone in Calcitta's alcoholic history. One of the earliest pubs in town, this place in park street is where a lot of us have started our drinking careers. It is not a clean, courteous, welcoming place where you can have a sophisticated drinking session in a calm & serene manner. But it is a place that celebrates this city's love for adda culture and indulges and embraces it heartily. Maybe that is the reason the place has seeped so deep into so many Calcuttan's fond memories and nostalgia and it continues to do so for the current generation as well inspite of all the rodents and cockroaches you might find crawling about.

If you are a newcomer willing to try the place for the first time, do remember the key phrase here is the charm. Not from the decor or the ambience (which are very average by today's standards) but from the feel and the diverse range of people around you being themselves. Its a melting pot and if you are interested in people and life and stories, you'll find those here.

The alcohol is cheap (but not the cheapest in the city) and the range of drinks available are the very basic. Do not expect exotic or high range drinks here. Popular demands rule. Try the Chicken ala kievs, mixed grills, the epynomous beef steaks or the liver masalas. They are inconsistent on a few occasions but on the average the food accompanied with the drinks are delicious and just perfect. 

The waiters can range from endearing to obnoxious depending upon the time of the evening and the amount of tip you decide to pay. You keep them happy and you can get away with almost anything :)

Rounding up, its not a place for everybody but if you are interested in the city and its people and its culture, do visit and spend a couple of hours here relaxing. Olypub has a knack of growing on you and enriching you with happy memories.

##

2014-03-24 16:29:14
Rishav Dey
193398
3.5
This review has been long pending, especially considering the number of times I have been to this place. Firstly one needs to understand clearly that Olypub is probably a B or C grade place but make no mistake it creates A grade memories each and every time one goes there. Each and every time has its own story. The place itself has an air of nostalgia about it. The attire of the waiters, the seating arrangement and the carpet on the AC floor but my favourite item of nostalgia is the peg measures of that the waiters use.
Talking of waiters, let me share a small anecdote. Once a friend, who is quite a character, referred to random waiters as Kaka. I said, "Chill, all tables have designated servers and ours is not around." His reply, "Dhur, chhar toh je mod debe shei Kaka." (Whoever serves alcohol can be referred to as Kaka.) Since then I have always called them Kaka.
The booze was once relatively cheap. Due to that reputation people continue to be under the impression that Olypub is still cheap. Now it is more or less on par with other places. The service is average and ambiance is variable, meaning that one is likely to find a different ambiance every day. Drink anything that you are in the mood for on that particular day and order anything that you like. I would recommend the cocktail sausages and the fish fingers. The steak although a big chunk of meat is way below par and is always overcooked. What matters more than anything else on Olypub is your company. And believe you me Olypub is best enjoyed when one lands up there randomly. 
Don't miss out on the charm of this place. This is one of the Kolkata heritages. But as I said make sure that you have good company and fun company.

Even the manager who sits downstairs once offered to click a pic of our gang together, wobbling on our way out one Christmas eve 9:30 pm! The waiters will never ever disturb you and you are allowed to stay as long you want but soberly so. I have seen them being stern with people who are sometimes rogue and loud, or are too inebriated. Such instances are rare and those noisemakers are politely ousted any way. The crowd is mostly young, decent and otherwise quite comfortable an atmosphere around here. Doesn't mean you bring your family tomorrow evening already! You can, but inform me before turning up okay? I promise we will be there, at the most glasses of vodka/beer crammed table- with chanachur and fries crumbs scattered all over.. We always sit upstairs at the extended wing on right, seriously!
Other than the superb location and ambiance, consider the following:
Pluses: Cheap booze, Beef Steak (Oly Pub ka steak nehi khaya toh kya khaya?), Mutton steak, chicken cutlet, Chicken a'la Kiev, smoking zone(NOT ANY MORE :( ), unlimited sitting hour with free chanachur if you can't afford anything solid!
(once we spent a full 5 hours, on a NYE)
Minuses: Sandwich and finger fries (just don't dare order, or do if you want a good intoxicated fit of laughter). Not all flavor variants of Breezers are available, nor your favorite cold drink will be there. We often had to select a second or a third choice from the alcohol options in the Menu. Smirnoff is not available some day, the next day they would say Volga isn't. Same goes with beer brands sometimes.

It's cheap and student friendly, who cares for the rest! Have a happy time :)

----- 09 Apr, 2013 -----

Okay, so first thing - I like the service here. If you guys are going to rant at me, go ahead. This place has a history of being one of the first places in Park Street I went to, and that too for the beef and the chicken liver. At Oly, you might see a cat suddenly peering at you from a tiny ventilator, or a group of random people bursting out singing all of a sudden. And oh, watch out for the times when the server tries to fleece you by adding up all the values already taxed, and then add a "special tax" to it. Thankfully, a bit of level-headedness can get you out of it, and when you need to chill with a bottle of beer, some good company and a plate of chicken sandwiches or a beefsteak, this is your baby.

Personal recommendation - go for the chicken liver, fried, after five in the evening.

2014-02-07 13:06:58
Esha Banerjee
79129
4.5
Its been 1.5 years since I first typed down a review for Olypub, just after my second visit there and I wrote as a distant observer.Over some time now, I have grown to love Oly (the fond nickname this place goes by), It is quintessentially Calcuttan, a cursory visit will not make it a experience, but keep coming back and you will get suffused in all its intimate charm.
The waiters will come to know you, they will flash a knowing smile when you order your drink, remember your table preferences,slip in a little chit chat : all the little things that makes memories.
The place, strictly speaking has no ambience.. the chatter of the people, and the odd toppa gaan from a veteran  makes up for it.
The drinks are  cheap,though i wish they would extend a larger selection.While the beef steak is not bad on some days, there are days it turns out to be hard and chewy, and I will never like the boiled peas that goes with it.My choice remains the chicken a la olypub.. batter fried chicken doused in creamy sauce served with butter fried bread..a calorie-laden bliss.You can go for the a la kiev too if super crusty chicken bomb with butter inside is your thing.. hate the cocktail sausages.Also this place is a real disaster if anyone chooses to go veg(like I did for some days ) : absolute dearth of options,the french fries were awful.
If you just let go off these small inconveniences, you will enjoy the  light-headed long discussions,  those evenings at Oly will tip-toe into your fond memory space.
As Vir Sanghvi famously proclaims: 'Calcutta grows on you', so does Oly.



----- 27 Oct, 2012 -----

Its good when you accept it as aplace to drink and chat,neither a family hangout or lovers hotspot,its best for a drink with friends.

The waiters are not polite,the service is a bit late,also they are pointy if you do not tip generously.
The food is ok sort of,the chicken omlette had very less stuffing and the beef steak-not bad,but it was boiled potatoes and not mashed potatoes that came along with it,the peas were boiled in water to a great degree thus taking away the fresh sweet taste,the onions were not chopped or fried well leading to a very unpleasant taste.Lastly do yourself a favor and do not order a lime soda.

2014-02-06 21:00:56
Chandreyee Mukherjee
789228
3.5
Olypub for some reason is a legend. The place where all my out of city friends wants to visit. When I end up taking them to Olypub invariably this is the questions that I get to hear after they are inside Oly..."so when are we going to Oly ?"

Well Oly is old. Scratch that. Oly is ancient. My dad used to frequent Oly when he just moved into the city in the early 70's. And I have been frequenting it from the past couple of years.

Food wise Oly is definitely not the greatest option in Park Street. Most people have a thing for their Beef Stake and the Mixed Grill. But they are both strictly okay. I personally like the Chicken Ala Olupub which is Oly's version of the Grilled Chicken and I also like their Chicken Fries which are thick batter friend pieces of chicken with their bones. THey also make a mean Tomato Omelette. Here I must also mention their Mustard(Kasundi). It is strong to say the least and I love it with everything served in Oly.

Drinks are cheap but basic. You will not get any fancy cocktails. Order your drinks with your juice or cold drinks or order your beer. The servers will come with a measuring peg and they do not really bother if some extra is just poured into your glass.

The servers are rather grumpy and like to dump the order on the table unceremoniously. Once I spilled some drinks on the table and had to incur the wrath of an Oly waiter. The servers also magically transform to jovial smiling friendly waiters when I end up in Oly with my very white, very blonde friend S.

The chairs are plastic and the tables are old sturdy white tables with various stains.Also I have personally seen rats in Oly and it is well known that they have a cat for the rats.

But still Oly is a legend. It is difficult to find a seat even in the middle of a week. It is buzzing with people from every age group, and conversation and laughter and arguments. I am not sure why it is a legend ? Maybe because it is one of the oldest Pub, maybe for the once delicious beef stake, maybe because of the people or maybe it is a legend just because it is a legend.

One certain afternoon after my office hours, I was in mood for some beer, which I had last while I was in college. Yes I am not much of a drinker but I like to dabble at times. So I grabbed a colleague from my work and made our way to Olypub. The ambiance was beautiful at best, though I failed to note any old world charm as is mentioned in some reviews.
On entering our way upstairs we sat at the corner-most table of the room on the right sight side. The waiter there seemed lost and disturbed which showed during the time when he came to get our order. 

I ordered a Heineken (beer) , Chicken cutlet, Masala Kulcha, Butter Naan and Chicken Masala. The spread tasted absolutely fantastic.The Indian breads deserve a special mention for being lucidly soft and light they were.The cutlet was good and so was the Chicken masala. I was still not full and wanted some more...i mean food. So I called back the waiter and he started mumbling something God knows what. Whatever, he took the last order which was a bottle of water and a Chicken Omelette.
The chicken omelette was again pretty tasty... so in all the food tasted better than average for me clubbed with the beautiful ambiance it was.

Finally after spending close to 2 hours we decided to leave and the pinch was not too deep @close to Rs.900/-. It's a beautiful place to visit even for the non-drinkers. So in my opinion a visit to this place is recommended at least once.

2013-12-28 00:31:57
.S.D.G.
116221
4.0
What can i say. Not accepting Credit cards takes a lot of courage under the hood. And they have it. Why? Because of their simply EXCEPTIONAL food. Its like a cult restaurant which has nothing more to prove to its thousand of fans.

Decor - Very Mediocre.
Food - Excellent (some special dishes which are not available anywhere else).
Service - good.
Crowd - Very laid back and relaxing.

Olypub Beef Steak has acquired a legendary status and righfully so. the tender meat with mashed potatoes and a poached egg on the top is something you will get addicted to. Compliment it with a bottle of Kingfisher and nothing else matters. You will be in food paradise. Smoking inside is allowed. So don't forget to carry a pack.

Chicken Olypub is their trademark dishe and it is definitely one of the best chicken preparation i have ever tasted. Soft chicken thigh meat with deep fried bread on a base a mashed potatoes loaded with butter and boiled peas.

Chicken Ala Kiev is a in house specialty. Its big balls of chicken deep fried with melting butter inside. Simple sinful addiction.


Have these 3 dishes along with beer. Trust me you will definitely visit again and become a part of the cult. A restaurant that was and always be one of kolkata's best hangouts.

Pricing -- Very cheap. for an idea, all the above and 3 beers would cost 600 bucks. 100 each.

Fish Fingers- The last time I ordered a plate, I did not find the fishes fresh enough leading to complete disappointment.

To pull it off finally, one can surely try this out for cheap booze and the crisp munchies and of course to feel the 'old nostalgia' but you can simply skip the option of ordering something that heavy.

Olypub on Park Street is perhaps the most popular watering hole for beasts like us. It serves no-nonsense food and alcohol at very easy-on-pocket prices, the service is laid back and environment loud. You will find the door open and close every 10 seconds as people either go out for a smoke or come in finishing one, not to mention the crowd that is always there. The chairs are old yet cosy although the sofas on the 1st floor could do with a bit of renovation. The tables are small, stout and firm and the waiters are all known by their first names. 

This is one of the few places in the city where you can have a beef steak and also serves excellent old style cocktail sausages, fish finger and finger chips. The boiled peas is a simple yet great starter and you can have a wide selection of alcohol- starting from beers to whiskey and rum and vodka.... the works. A nice, laid back, old world charm envelopes the place and one can actually sit there alone and soak in the ambience. A great place no doubt.

Do not expect fine ambience at Olypub. Firstly, it is not posh. Prices are pretty moderate. I mean 70/-  for one pint of beer is way affordable, that too in an area like Park Street.
Olypub has its own crowd which often is not very polished and I am not a racist :P

Just being honest. Olypub can give you a good time over steaks and beer with friends. Its a NO for family outings.
It is usually buzzing with people and yes its just basic clean and decent. Nothing great so do not have high expectations from this place.

But for leisure, yes I would suggest :)
Its is VERY easy on the pockets. So do not think twice before visiting but a big NO for posh freaks! 

Cheers!

2013-11-03 21:15:03
Debdeep Banerjee

3.5
Olypub is the place to be, if you are looking for a quick booze at Park Street.

A lot of nostalgia, drunken-ness and beef steak, thats olypub in a nutshell.
The booze here is cheaper than any other place in Park Street, hence college go-ers find instant solitude inside. The menu isn't too extensive but there are a few items that you can certainly look in to. 
 
Chick-A-La Kiev is served at Olypub and is one of the best things that you finnd here, chicken deep fried in a pretty battter, with  butter oozing out as you take a bite. A perfect compliment for your drink.
The Beef steak, is perhaps the best beef steak that you get in the city. The portion of beef is large and the steak is grilled to perfection. It is soft and full of flavour. It is served with steamed peas, mashed potatoes and mushroom, thus providing a proper texture. Altogether at the given price, it is a must must try!

Apart from these two, you can also try the Chilli fish, the fresh fish is sure to appeal to your taste buds. 
People come to Olypub to drink and get high, but Olypub can get you high without spirit if you know what to order. So grab your drink, or a bottle of beer, order food and Bottoms up!

##

2013-09-21 21:18:30
Subhasish Das
2646
3.5
27June 2014
Recently tried their Fish finger and Chicken Ala Kiev. I really liked both these dishes and tasted pretty much like it used to taste several years back. The service we got around 11 at night was also very decent. Hence revising the rating to 3.5 :) 

----------
I believe that Olypub is one of the most primitive watering holes in Calcutta. It has served to quite a few famous personalities from Bengal and elsewhere. Olypub is as famous as its patrons but unfortunately all these things are of the past. I used to be a regular here during my college days though my college was not anywhere near Park Street, but me and my friends always used to hang out at Olypub for few drinks before or after hitting Someplace else for a gig (usually Cassinis Division or Hip Pocket). Gone are those days .. sigh.!! 
Recently visited olypub after a very long time and sadly loads have changed. The staff has changed, the ambiance and crowd is not exuberant anymore.
Located just beside the Park Hotel, Olypub is spread into two floors. The ground floor used to be the stags section and the 1st floor used to be a family section (if you have a lady as a company), but I guess that rule does not apply any more as we saw a ladies group seated downstairs. Ambiance is nothing to write home about. Its just the pre historic charm that brings me back to the place. To be frank, the decor and seating is pretty shabby. During peak rush hours, you might be asked to share a table with fellow diners. On weekends the place is packed right from afternoon.  I visited around 3 pm and it was packed ! 
Food and Drinks : Olypub is a basically a place to drink where food takes a back seat ! Drinks are cheap, at least the cheapest in Park Street Area. A 650ml bottle of beer(Tuborg) is priced around Rs138. Whisky - 60ml (Signature) is priced at Rs118. White Rum is priced at Rs98. Best part is that the drinks are poured right in front of you from the respective bottles in proper peg measures!! 
Olypub used to be famous for its Beef Stake, the chicken Ala kiev and the Mixed Grill. Unfortunately none of them taste the same. Atleast Beef stake and Chicken Ala kiev is not the same anymore. You may try it but for people who used to be regulars out here several years back will be majorly disappointed ! Food is priced reasonably and the price ranges from Rs 100-200. But the munchies mixture that is accompanied with  the drinks is still my favourite ! :) 
Service: The service has gone down as well. The waiters(chachas as we used to call them) have changed. They expect a large tip all the time and you need to keep them reminding about the food order otherwise they are most likely to forget ! Also, Cash is the only mode of payment which is a big negative ! 
Keeping aside so many negatives, I will be back to Olypub with my friends to re live my college days and enjoy cheap drinks and nostalgia at the heart of Park Street ... forgetting everything else in the world !

##

2013-07-25 13:08:29
Shubham Basu
924648
3.5
Once upon a time, Olypub was known as the Mecca of drinks on Park Street. It was here that college goers and young people would come to enjoy the cheap drinks and good food. Sadly, that era is a thing of the past now. The present day Olypub retains its interiors just as it was 10 years ago, but the service and the food has become a huge let-down, which has led many of its loyal customers to seek haven at the Trincas bar just next door. 

 I visited Olypub last Sunday with three friends. The doorman told us there was no available seats on the first floor (which could be expected, since it was after all, the weekend), but we went up anyway to wait. To our surprise, there were MANY seats that were empty, so we easily got seated. Funny how the doorman himself didn't know if places were available or not. We ordered the Chicken A La Kiev,  Mixed Grill, Chateaubriand Steak, Chilli Mutton, and Fish Reshmi Kabab, along with a host of drinks. Now the first minus point of Olypub is that, the drinks arrive in a minute, but one has to wait over 30 minutes for the food. So, as I noticed, either one has to wait till the food arrives to start their drinks, or re-order drinks when the food is served. We sat there, sipping soft drinks till our food was served to us. The chicken A La Kiev did have warm butter drizzling out of it, but we struggled to find chicken in the dish. It was mostly the bread and potato stuffing which made up the cutlet, giving it a bland flavour. The Mixed Grill, Chilli Mutton and Chateaubriand steak all had the same flavour base, which was hilarious. And what can I say about the Chateaubriand Steak?? This steak, which was once soft and succulent, easy to cut and chew, had the texture of rubber. All four of us struggled to chew it down. The mashed potato served with it was just plain boiled potato which did not even have salt in it. Same goes for the peas, which were simply boiled. The only saviour was the Fish Kabab, which was soft, flavorful and delicious.

In conclusion, if you wish to have a few drinks with your friends at cheap prices in a posh area like Park Street, Olypub is the place to go. But if you are hungry, this once famous place is not the place to be.

3.0
The first thing you notice about this institution on Park Street is the stench of stale beer and what might possibly be puke.
But its the best place in the city to booze, with friends. You'll not even realize how time passes by! The booze is cheap. The food is okay. 
The first time i visited Oly, was actually for the Beef Steak and not the beer. Their Chateau Briand (glorified beef steak ;) ) was once really good. They served it with mashed potatoes,and steamed veggies. Also they serve a special mustard sauce that goes really well with it.
But the quality of the beef steak has gone down. Really down. It's now a fraction of the size it used to be, mostly very tough and excessively chewy. It's not something I would recommend anymore.
Their mixed grill is pretty good.
But, it's a pub. Somewhere you go to drink with friends and have fun, or to drown your sorrows in alcohol, and as a pub it scores pretty well.
Go there for the cheap booze and the all round experience. Not the Food.
Recommended.

2013-07-08 14:14:18
Sanjana Bhattacharyya
235009
2.0
I don't know what makes people speak very pretentiously of Olypub, but I can say from experience, it is far from the posh and cozy little pub I had expected it to be. Also, all you want from this place is a good beef steak, then do head somewhere else because it is utter disappointment.

One wintry afternoon, a bunch of us headed to Olypub to have a nosh and a tipple with high expectations. A couple of us ordered the much talked about Chateaubriand, while a few ordered the Chicken a la Kiev and the rest stuck to Chicken Butter Masala and Butter Naan. I have never been to a restaurant before where they fail so wholesomely that there's not a single good thing I can write about. The a la Kiev tasted too bready, and you know right away that there's as much bread in the cutlets as chicken. The Butter Masala too was ordinary. 

As for the beef steak, the less said, the better. The measly amount of potato mash, only a couple of slices of mushroom served along with it were disappointing. But that is nothing compared to what I experienced when I tried slicing the steak. It was tough as hide! There was barely a tablespoon of sauce on the steak and when I did manage to carve (and tear and bite) a slice off the steak, I took about five minutes to chew it into a tendon-y mush that could not be disintegrated further. My jaw was aching by the time I could finish. Never again. I'd rather have beef roll from dingy looking eateries than try another steak here.

To top it all off, the waiters were rude, lazy and actually had the gall to ask for a larger tip! How posh is that!

I think I managed to give this place 2 (after much deliberation, I must add) because the vodka soda highball was the highlight of my meal. But that's probably because the pub had nothing to do with its making, Vodka and soda were both manufactured products and we made the highball by proportioning the liquids.

Fifth, if you want to take a fag drag then there's a small crowded space in the way to the washroom where you can do it.
At the end, all the above points won't bother you anymore when you leave this place, 
satisfied with your drink and contented with the time spent among your good old buddies.

Immediately after I left without wanting to experiment even more and to move to other places in the area. A whole in all a bitter experience for me in a city I'd come to admire for the food.

Good but dubious food at Olypub!
3 out of 5

Enjoying good food at a popular restaurant is great, but you cannot judge a restaurant by its decor and style until you taste its food, just as you cannot judge a book by its cover until you've read it. 

My experience of eating at Olypub was somewhat mixed. I had no plans of eating at Olypub. But, yes I was in Park Street to dine at a popular restaurant. It was the weekend and Park Street was full of food lovers, ready to gorge on lip smacking delicacies offered at the various restaurants here which is why everything was full. I waited for forty-five minutes at Peter Cat but with no hope of getting a table for myself, I decided to dine at another restaurant in Park Street and settled for Olypub.  

Frankly speaking, I was not quite impressed by its decor and ambience. The service was satisfactory, but they could really improve on it. As I was hungry, I ignored the poor service and decided to concentrate on the food. I ordered Cream of Chicken Soup,  Hamburger Steak (mutton) and Chicken a la Kiev (my favourite). The quality of food served at Olypub is awesome and quantity is good as well. 

I knew I could not finish everything alone and requested the waiter to pack some for home. I enjoyed the flavours of the Chicken Soup and loved the Kiev. I also enjoyed the Hamburger Steak (mutton), which was appetizing but a tad undercooked. 

After a very long time, I actually enjoyed some good continental food in a restaurant. I am looking forward to a second visit to Olypub. You may not like the ambience or their standards of hygiene, but believe me you'll enjoy the food there.

After reading all the reviews on Zomato I finally decided to go check it out myself. Quite honestly? I'm disappointed, and this is after I visited the place twice. The place is at best mediocre when it comes to continental food which people quite fondly review here. If the steak here is considered the best in town, I wonder how people in Kolkata judge steaks. The booze is definitely cheap for an establishment in a place like Park Street. Is it an attraction? No it is not. But be sure to drop in if you're Park Street and are hungry and low on money.

2013-01-26 15:35:23
Abhirup Chakrabarty
497149
4.5
Well, ahem, let me clear a thing or two at the very first chance. I have been a Oly Pub fanatic since the last 8-9 years or so and will continue to be one no matter how shady, rude, pathetic and indifferent they become. It will always have a special place in my heart for providing me and my friends with innumerable wonderful memories over the years.

Now, to the point. 
It serves liquor at the cheapest rates in & around Park Street area. 
It serves very very well cooked Beef Steak, Chicken A-la-Kiev and other continental dishes. In fact, I have ordered Beef Steak each and every time I have visited there. Never have I been disappointed with that particular dish.
It is the ultimate place to chill out with every type (school/college/office/para) of buddies.
It won't burn a hole in your pocket with its bill (although rates have skyrocketed in the last two years, coupled with exorbitant taxes).
Gossip, sing, shout, dance (Ok, I am going overboard) at your own will.
The service at times can be pretty pathetic with waiters being rude, but being a regular for so many years definitely helps ;) . (Yes, they would give preference to old timers. So, freshers beware :) )
There are plenty of mice running around here and there under the shredded carpets and yes, at times with cats chasing after them. Free entertainment, you see ;)
Ambiance. Well, if you are the finicky types and swear by neatness, cleanliness et all, please stay 1000 miles away from this pub. However, you can meet up with the most peculiar of the personalities of Kolkata in Oly Pub. My experiences range from the usual drunkards to intense philosophical discussions, musical evenings, heated arguments, emotional outbursts, fistfights and smashing bottles to even a random French guy singing "Ami chini go chini tomare ogo bideshini". You get the drift I presume.
So, all in all, this is definitely not for persons with weak heart or with cleanliness issues. For others - Two Thumbs Up - Be sure to complete your pilgrimage by visiting Oly.

4.5 stars from me.

2013-01-04 17:27:48
Kuhelika Guha
285787
4.0
I wonder what I should begin with when talking about one of THE institutions of Kolkata. So, I've decided to begin with the #Caution: "All mild hearted people, visit at your own risk". This isn't a place for the fussy but definitely a place for the fun loving.

Situated in the heart of Park Street, this shady little pub has been a haunt for students, media people and just about everyone else forever, and it isn't uncommon to wind up in a queue for a table. Oly Pub is shady in every sense of the word, from its ragged carpets to spindly tables and cob webs to the old school waiters who seem to be more drunk that the customers! This place is fantastic! My favorite bit is when the waiter places the water on your table in a old glass country whiskey bottle and some 'chakna' with it.

The place has becoming non-smoking of late (except for the balcony near the loo) and shuts down at 10.30 (thank you Momota Didi), but has still kept is price-list nearly the same (cheap!). A bottle of kingfisher cost around 150 bucks which is damn good considering you're in Park Street.

The food is also reasonably priced, however, a lot of people I know don't like eating here as they suspect the food to be unhygienic! #Mind you here, I am from Delhi and I've eaten absolutely gorgeous food at Oly plenty of times and never gotten a bug! The Chicken Liver Fry and Mix Grill Platter are to die for! The Mix Grill Platter has an assortment of chicken, liver, beef and pork in a yummy sauce topped with a half fry egg. Its one of the most gorgeous things I've ever tasted and up there in my Bucket List for others to try. And yes, I say again that it's all really economical.

RECOMMENDED with all my heart and taste-buds!

Visited the place after ages.It was nice to see that the place hasn't changed a bit over the years.Tradition of pouring the drink from the bottle in front of the customer,payment by cash ONLY,strictly ordinary food, same style of glasses for every type of drink and dirt cheap prices. Smirnoff-60 ml for Rs 104/-.So you know what i mean!!!Easily the cheapest prices for drinks in Kolkata.No wonder that the place was jam packed with mostly teenagers and the seniors were seriously outnumbered.People were waiting at the staircase for a table-Saturday evening, thus understandable.
Among the food items the chicken reshmi kebab,mixed grill and fish finger was okay.Fried chicken and chilly mutton was horrendous-too spicy for consumption.Avoid these items.Heard the steak(beef/mutton) is still pretty good and popular but did not try it.

The roast mutton was tender and came with house fries and veggies,  not the crappy freezer chips.  

If u like steaks,  theirs comes with a poached egg on top.  But it's well done .  

Saving the best for the last.  The house mustard.  I  fell in love with it.  Slathered the chicken livers with it and it was pure ecstatic.  

The newly done up interiors are nice and the staff was warm and courteous.  

Cheers to old world charm.

2011-08-21 23:12:41
Jashadip Datta
29563
3.0
Nothings changed about the place from the day I first visited it, on recommendations from various elder brotherly quarters...
Its the same waiters, in the same maroon liveries, serving the mixed grills and steaks and ... it still serves the most affordable liquor along the stretch of Park Street! Cheers!

I like the way they pour my poison right in front of me. It kinds of builds up the zest for a tipple.
The servicing may seem to be a bit rude if one is not used to the place, but personally I feel they operate on a known face, repeat customer basis. Anyways they don't tend to intrude 
at anytime and are least bothered if you chat away with your friends for a really long time without ordering anything.

Often the beef steak of Olypub has been praised. But personally I find that they tend to overcook the beef. 
The Mixed Grill platter on the other hand is something that I order regularly and it actually goes quite well with the liquor. Other food items on the menu list are quite agreeable and definitely worth the moderate price tag that they command.
If someone is looking for a laid back relaxed time with friends without hurting the pocket much and in the process look into something which has garnered a reputation for itself over decades...then this is the place to be.

Overall:
F & B: 3.5 out of 5 
Service: 3 out of 5
Ambiance: 3.5 out of 5

##

2011-01-06 12:53:14
Tulleeho!
13993
4.0
January last, on a visit through Calcutta, I made my obligatory pilgrimage to Olypub, and noted with relief that it had remained mostly unchanged and stood resolutely uncompromised by the terrible beauties thrown up by our current soulless age. Still located on Park Street, a stone's throw away from Trinca's, the famous night club of yore, the ambience and the familiar dilapidation of the building remain the same, a distinction not many institutions can boast of in these murderously exhilarating times of consumer preferences with their insistence on tasteless packaging and grotesque upgradations to theme pubs and discotheqes.The place opens at 11:00 am and the narrow side annexe to the older main establishment, Olympia Bar, leads to steep, rickety steps which display no embarrassment at the cheap and frayed coir matting adorning them, before opening out into the low-ceilinged mezzanine floor which constitutes the bar proper and which is further subdivided into two sections, connected by a stair of 4/5 steps.

Read the complete review on <a target="_blank" href="http://www.tulleeho.com/bc/bar1.asp?ID=46">Tulleeho!</a>
